async function loadOrders(){


const response=await fetch(

"https://saybon-backend.onrender.com/admin/orders"

);


const data=await response.json();


const table=

document.querySelector("#ordersTable tbody");


data.orders.forEach(order=>{


const row=document.createElement("tr");


row.innerHTML=`

<td>${order.email}</td>

<td>${order.filename}</td>

<td>${order.words}</td>

<td>$${order.price}</td>

<td>${order.status}</td>

<td>

<a href="${order.fileUrl}" target="_blank">

Download

</a>

</td>

`;


table.appendChild(row);


});


}


loadOrders();

import dotenv from "dotenv";

/*
========================================
LOAD ENV FIRST (ABSOLUTE TOP)
========================================
*/
dotenv.config({ path: "./.env" });

/*
========================================
IMPORTS
========================================
*/
import express from "express";
import cors from "cors";

import requestRoutes from "./routes/requestRoutes.js";
import stripeRoutes from "./routes/stripeRoutes.js";
import paystackRoutes from "./routes/paystackRoutes.js";

/*
========================================
INIT
========================================
*/
const app = express();

/*
========================================
MIDDLEWARE
========================================
*/
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

/*
========================================
HEALTH CHECK
========================================
*/
app.get("/", (req, res) => {
  res.send("SayBon Backend Running");
});

/*
========================================
ROUTES (CANONICAL API)
========================================
- Quote upload + word count:
  POST /api/quote   (multipart form-data "file")

- Stripe session:
  POST /api/stripe/create-stripe-session  (json {amount})

- Paystack init:
  POST /api/paystack/initialize           (json {amount, email})
========================================
*/
app.use("/api/quote", requestRoutes);
app.use("/api/stripe", stripeRoutes);
app.use("/api/paystack", paystackRoutes);

/*
========================================
LEGACY ALIASES (so old frontend links still work)
========================================
*/
app.use("/request", requestRoutes);
app.use("/stripe", stripeRoutes);
app.use("/paystack", paystackRoutes);

/*
========================================
404
========================================
*/
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({
    success: false,
    message: "Endpoint not found"
  });
});

/*
========================================
SERVER
========================================
*/
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

app.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log("SayBon backend running on port " + PORT);
});

/**
 * SayBon Payments API (Firebase Functions v2)
 * Route:
 * POST /api/create-stripe-session
 */

// force redeploy

const { onRequest } = require("firebase-functions/v2/https");
const express = require("express");
const cors = require("cors");

try { require("dotenv").config(); } catch (e) {}

const Stripe = require("stripe");

const app = express();

app.use(cors({ origin: true }));
app.use(express.json({ limit: "1mb" }));

function mustEnv(name) {
  const v = process.env[name];
  if (!v) throw new Error(`Missing environment variable: ${name}`);
  return v;
}

function safeNumber(n, fallback = 0) {
  const x = Number(n);
  return Number.isFinite(x) ? x : fallback;
}

function clampInt(n, min, max) {
  const x = Math.round(safeNumber(n, min));
  return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, x));
}

function normalizeCurrency(cur) {
  const c = String(cur || "USD").trim().toUpperCase();
  if (["USD","GBP","EUR"].includes(c)) return c;
  return "USD";
}

function formatPlan(plan) {
  const p = String(plan || "").toLowerCase();
  return p === "express" ? "express" : "standard";
}

/* ===============================
   STRIPE CHECKOUT
================================ */

app.post("/create-stripe-session", async (req,res) => {

  try {

const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY);
    const currency = normalizeCurrency(req.body.currency);
    const plan = formatPlan(req.body.plan);

    const words = clampInt(req.body.words,1,5000000);
    const amount = safeNumber(req.body.amount,0);

    const amountCents = clampInt(amount * 100,50,500000000);

    const origin = req.headers.origin || "https://saybonapp.com";

    const session = await stripe.checkout.sessions.create({

      mode:"payment",

      line_items:[{
        price_data:{
          currency:currency.toLowerCase(),
          product_data:{
            name: plan === "express" ? "Express Translation" : "Standard Translation",
            description:`${words} words`
          },
          unit_amount:amountCents
        },
        quantity:1
      }],

      success_url:`${origin}/translation/success.html?session_id={CHECKOUT_SESSION_ID}`,

      cancel_url:`${origin}/translation/request.html`

    });

    res.json({ url: session.url });

  }

  catch(err){

    console.error("Stripe error:",err);

    res.status(400).json({
      error:"stripe_error",
      message:err.message
    });

  }

});

/* ===============================
   HEALTH CHECK
================================ */

app.get("/health",(req,res)=>{
  res.json({ ok:true });
});

/* ===============================
   EXPORT API
================================ */

exports.api = onRequest({

  region:"us-central1",

  secrets:[
    "STRIPE_SECRET_KEY"
  ]

},app);

/* force redeploy 11 Mar */

import express from "express";
import cors from "cors";
import Stripe from "stripe";
import admin from "firebase-admin";

const app = express();

/* ==========================================
FIREBASE ADMIN
========================================== */

admin.initializeApp();
const db = admin.firestore();

/* ==========================================
STRIPE INITIALIZATION
========================================== */

const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY,{
  apiVersion:"2023-10-16"
});

/* ==========================================
WEBHOOK (RAW BODY REQUIRED)
========================================== */

app.post("/webhook", express.raw({type:"application/json"}), async (req,res)=>{

  let event;

  try{

    event = stripe.webhooks.constructEvent(
      req.body,
      req.headers["stripe-signature"],
      process.env.STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET
    );

  }catch(err){

    console.error("Webhook signature verification failed:",err.message);
    return res.status(400).send(`Webhook Error: ${err.message}`);

  }

  /* ==========================================
  PAYMENT COMPLETED
  ========================================== */

  if(event.type === "checkout.session.completed"){

    const session = event.data.object;
    const jobId = session.client_reference_id;

    console.log("Stripe payment received for job:",jobId);

    if(jobId){

      try{

        await db.collection("translationJobs")
        .doc(jobId)
        .update({
          status:"paid",
          paidAt:new Date()
        });

        console.log("Firestore updated for:",jobId);

      }catch(err){

        console.error("Firestore update failed:",err);

      }

    }

  }

  res.json({received:true});

});

/* ==========================================
MIDDLEWARE (AFTER WEBHOOK)
========================================== */

app.use(cors({
  origin:[
    "https://saybonapp.com",
    "http://localhost:5500"
  ],
  methods:["GET","POST"],
  allowedHeaders:["Content-Type"]
}));

app.use(express.json());

/* ==========================================
SERVER HEALTH CHECK
========================================== */

app.get("/", (req,res)=>{
  res.json({
    status:"SayBon server running"
  });
});

/* ==========================================
CREATE STRIPE CHECKOUT
========================================== */

app.post("/api/createCheckout", async (req,res)=>{

  try{

    const { words, plan, jobId } = req.body;

    if(!words || !plan || !jobId){
      return res.status(400).json({
        error:"Missing words, plan or jobId"
      });
    }

    let price = 0;

    if(plan==="express"){
      price = words * 0.05;
    }else{
      price = words * 0.025;
    }

    const session = await stripe.checkout.sessions.create({

      payment_method_types:["card"],

      mode:"payment",

      line_items:[{
        price_data:{
          currency:"usd",
          product_data:{
            name:"SayBon Translation Service"
          },
          unit_amount:Math.round(price * 100)
        },
        quantity:1
      }],

      client_reference_id: jobId,

      metadata:{
        words:String(words),
        plan:String(plan)
      },

      success_url:
      "https://saybonapp.com/translation/success.html?job="+jobId,

      cancel_url:
      "https://saybonapp.com/translation/request.html"

    });

    res.json({
      url:session.url
    });

  }catch(err){

    console.error("Stripe Checkout Error:",err);

    res.status(500).json({
      error:"Stripe checkout failed"
    });

  }

});

/* ==========================================
404 HANDLER
========================================== */

app.use((req,res)=>{
  res.status(404).json({
    error:"Route not found"
  });
});

/* ==========================================
START SERVER (RENDER)
========================================== */

const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

app.listen(PORT, ()=>{
  console.log("SayBon payment server running on port", PORT);
});

import fs from "fs";

export default async function(req,res){

try{

const file=req.file;

if(!file){

return res.status(400).json({

error:"No file"

});

}

const text=fs.readFileSync(file.path,"utf8");

const words=text.trim().split(/\s+/).length;

res.json({

wordCount:words,

standard:(words*0.025).toFixed(2),

express:(words*0.05).toFixed(2)

});

}catch(e){

res.status(500).json({

error:e.message

});

}

}

rules_version = '2';

service cloud.firestore {

match /databases/{database}/documents {

function isSignedIn() {
return request.auth != null;
}

function isOwner(userId) {
return request.auth != null && request.auth.uid == userId;
}

/* USERS */

match /users/{userId} {
allow read, write: if isOwner(userId);
}

/* TRANSLATION REQUESTS */

match /translationRequests/{doc} {
allow read, write: if isSignedIn();
}

/* TRANSLATOR TESTS */

match /translatorTests/{doc} {
allow read, write: if isSignedIn();
}

/* TRANSLATOR APPLICATIONS */

match /translatorApplications/{doc} {
allow read: if isSignedIn();
allow write: if isSignedIn();
}

/* ADMIN COLLECTION */

match /admin/{doc} {
allow read, write: if false;
}

}
}

rules_version = '2';

service firebase.storage {

match /b/{bucket}/o {

function signedIn() {
return request.auth != null;
}

/* USER UPLOADS */

match /userUploads/{userId}/{allPaths=**} {
allow read, write: if request.auth != null && request.auth.uid == userId;
}

/* TRANSLATION DOCUMENTS */

match /translations/{allPaths=**} {
allow read, write: if signedIn();
}

/* DEFAULT BLOCK */

match /{allPaths=**} {
allow read, write: if false;
}

}
}

export async function deliverTranslation(db,jobId,translation){

const jobRef=db.collection("translationJobs").doc(jobId);

const jobDoc=await jobRef.get();

if(!jobDoc.exists){
throw new Error("Job not found");
}

await jobRef.update({

status:"completed",
finalTranslation:translation,
deliveredAt:new Date()

});

return{
delivered:true
};

}

===========================================
FILE: engine\job-allocation.js
===========================================

export async function acceptJob(db,jobId,translatorId){

const jobRef=db.collection("translationJobs").doc(jobId);

const jobDoc=await jobRef.get();

if(!jobDoc.exists){
throw new Error("Job not found");
}

let job=jobDoc.data();

if(job.acceptedCount>=3){
throw new Error("Job already closed");
}

const acceptRef=db.collection("jobAcceptances");

const existing=await acceptRef
.where("jobId","==",jobId)
.where("translatorId","==",translatorId)
.get();

if(!existing.empty){
throw new Error("Translator already accepted job");
}

await acceptRef.add({

jobId:jobId,
translatorId:translatorId,
acceptedAt:new Date()

});

await jobRef.update({

acceptedCount:job.acceptedCount+1

});

return{
accepted:true
};

}

===========================================
FILE: engine\job-engine.js
===========================================

export async function acceptJob(db,jobId,translatorId){

const jobRef=db.collection("translationJobs").doc(jobId);
const doc=await jobRef.get();

let job=doc.data();

let accepted=job.acceptedTranslators||[];

if(accepted.includes(translatorId))
return {message:"already accepted"};

if(accepted.length>=3)
return {message:"job closed"};

accepted.push(translatorId);

await jobRef.update({
acceptedTranslators:accepted,
status:"in_progress"
});

return {success:true};

}

FILE: engine\payout-engine.js

export function calculatePayout(position,score){

if(score<85) return 0;

if(position===1) return 1.0;
if(position===2) return 0.4;
if(position===3) return 0.2;

return 0;

}

import OpenAI from "openai";

const openai = new OpenAI({
apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY
});

export async function evaluateTranslation(source,translation){

try{

const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({

model:"gpt-4o-mini",

temperature:0.2,

messages:[

{
role:"system",
content:`You are a professional translation reviewer. 
Score the translation quality from 0 to 100.
Return JSON with score and feedback.`
},

{
role:"user",
content:`
SOURCE TEXT:

${source}

TRANSLATION:

${translation}

Evaluate:

1 accuracy
2 grammar
3 meaning preservation
4 completeness

Return JSON format:

{
score: number,
feedback: "short explanation"
}
`
}

]

});

const content=response.choices[0].message.content;

return JSON.parse(content);

}catch(err){

console.error("QUALITY CHECK ERROR",err);

return {
score:0,
feedback:"AI evaluation failed"
};

}

}

===========================================
FILE: engine\reputation-engine.js
===========================================

export async function updateReputation(db,translatorId,score,onTime){

const ref=db.collection("translatorProfiles").doc(translatorId);

const doc=await ref.get();

if(!doc.exists) return;

let data=doc.data();

let jobsSubmitted=data.jobsSubmitted+1;

let jobsPassed=data.jobsPassed;
let jobsRejected=data.jobsRejected;

if(score>=85){
jobsPassed++;
}else{
jobsRejected++;
}

let averageScore=((data.averageScore*(jobsSubmitted-1))+score)/jobsSubmitted;

let completionRate=jobsPassed/jobsSubmitted;

let onTimeRate=((data.onTimeRate*(jobsSubmitted-1))+(onTime?1:0))/jobsSubmitted;

let reputation=

(averageScore*0.6)+
(completionRate*100*0.3)+
(onTimeRate*100*0.1);

await ref.update({

jobsSubmitted,
jobsPassed,
jobsRejected,
averageScore,
onTimeRate,
reputationScore:reputation

});

}

===========================================
FILE: engine\segmenter.js
===========================================

export function segmentText(text){

const maxWords=900;

const words=text.split(" ");

let segments=[];
let current=[];

for(let word of words){

current.push(word);

if(current.length>=maxWords){

segments.push(current.join(" "));
current=[];

}

}

if(current.length>0){

segments.push(current.join(" "));

}

return segments;

}

===========================================
FILE: engine\segment-translate.js
===========================================

import { segmentText } from "./segmenter.js";
import { translateText } from "./ai-translation.js";

export async function translateLargeDocument(text,sourceLang,targetLang){

const segments=segmentText(text);

let translatedSegments=[];

for(const segment of segments){

const translated=await translateText(segment,sourceLang,targetLang);

translatedSegments.push(translated);

}

return translatedSegments.join("\n\n");

}

===========================================
FILE: engine\translation-memory.js
===========================================

export async function saveTranslationMemory(db,source,target,sourceLang,targetLang){

if(!source || !target) return;

await db.collection("translationMemory").add({

source:source.trim(),
target:target.trim(),
sourceLang:sourceLang,
targetLang:targetLang,
createdAt:new Date()

});

}



export async function applyTranslationMemory(db,text){

const snapshot = await db.collection("translationMemory").get();

let output=text;

snapshot.forEach(doc=>{

const memory=doc.data();

if(memory.source && memory.target){

const regex=new RegExp(memory.source,"gi");

output=output.replace(regex,memory.target);

}

});

return output;

}

===========================================
FILE: index.js

const functions = require("firebase-functions/v2/https");
const admin = require("firebase-admin");

admin.initializeApp();

exports.api = functions.onRequest(async (req, res) => {

  try {

    // Health test
    if (req.method === "GET") {
      res.json({ status: "SayBon API running" });
      return;
    }

    // Order creation
    if (req.body.type === "order") {

      const order = {

        email: req.body.email,
        amount: req.body.amount,
        currency: req.body.currency,
        status: "paid",
        created: Date.now()

      };

      await admin.firestore()
        .collection("translationOrders")
        .add(order);

      res.json({
        ok: true
      });

      return;

    }

    res.status(400).json({
      error: "Invalid request"
    });

  }

  catch (error) {

    res.status(500).json({
      error: error.message
    });

  }

});

const firebaseConfig={
apiKey:"YOUR_API_KEY",
authDomain:"YOUR_PROJECT.firebaseapp.com",
projectId:"YOUR_PROJECT"
}

firebase.initializeApp(firebaseConfig)

const db=firebase.firestore()

db.collection("jobs")
.onSnapshot(snap=>{

let html=""

snap.forEach(doc=>{
const j=doc.data()

html+=`
<div>
<b>${j.jobCode}</b> � ${j.status}
</div>
`
})

document.getElementById("jobs").innerHTML=html

})

</script>

FILE: public\admin\passkey\passkey.js
===========================================

(async function () {
  const input = document.getElementById("passkeyInput");
  const button = document.getElementById("unlockBtn");
  const status = document.getElementById("status");

  async function validate() {
    const key = (input.value || "").trim();

    if (!key) {
      status.textContent = "Enter a valid passkey.";
      return;
    }

    status.textContent = "Checking clearance...";

    try {
      const res = await fetch("/data/admin-clearances.json", { cache: "no-store" });
      const records = await res.json();

      const matched = Array.isArray(records)
        ? records.find(r => r.enabled === true && String(r.passkey).trim() === key)
        : null;

      if (!matched) {
        status.textContent = "Access denied.";
        return;
      }

      localStorage.setItem("saybon_admin_clearance", JSON.stringify(matched));
      window.location.href = "/admin/access-granted/";
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      status.textContent = "Could not verify clearance.";
    }
  }

  button.addEventListener("click", validate);
  input.addEventListener("keydown", (e) => {
    if (e.key === "Enter") validate();
  });
})();

async function loadJobs(){

const response = await fetch("/api/editor/jobs");

const jobs = await response.json();

const container = document.getElementById("jobs");

container.innerHTML="";

jobs.forEach(job=>{

const div = document.createElement("div");

div.className="job";

</button>

});

FILE: public\dashboard\dashboard.js
===========================================

// ============================
// DASHBOARD ROUTING — CLEAN & SAFE
// ============================

// ---------- ROUTE FUNCTIONS ----------

function goLevels() {
  window.location.href = "../levels/index.html";
}

function goTalkletics() {
  window.location.href = "../games/index.html";
}

function goMusic() {
  window.location.href = "../music/index.html";
}

function goDelf() {
  window.location.href = "../delf/index.html";
}

function goTranslation() {
  window.location.href = "../translation/index.html";
}

function goChat() {
  window.location.href = "../chat/index.html";
}

function goFeedback() {
  window.location.href = "../features/feedback/index.html";
}

function goSupport() {
  window.location.href = "../support/index.html";
}

function goHome() {
  window.location.href = "../index.html";
}


// ============================
// ICON INTERACTION SYSTEM
// ============================

// Map icon keys to route functions
const routeMap = {
  levels: goLevels,
  games: goTalkletics,
  music: goMusic,
  delf: goDelf,
  translation: goTranslation,
  chat: goChat
};

let lastTapped = null;

document.querySelectorAll(".icon-item").forEach(icon => {

  const key = icon.dataset.key; // IMPORTANT: must match HTML

  icon.addEventListener("click", function () {

    // DESKTOP: navigate instantly
    if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
      routeMap[key]();
      return;
    }

    // MOBILE: double tap logic
    if (lastTapped === this) {
      routeMap[key]();
    } else {
      // Hide all labels
      document.querySelectorAll(".label").forEach(l => {
        l.style.opacity = 0;
      });

      // Show this label
      this.querySelector(".label").style.opacity = 1;

      lastTapped = this;
    }

  });

});

import { initializeApp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js";
import {
  getAuth,
  GoogleAuthProvider,
  signInWithPopup
} from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-auth.js";

const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey: "AIzaSyB2aKUdE1NSt0kN332BwTYSX52D0lxj1g0",
  authDomain: "saybon-3e3c2.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId: "saybon-3e3c2",
  storageBucket: "saybon-3e3c2.appspot.com",
  messagingSenderId: "75085012344",
  appId: "1:75085012344:web:0b18581cb0a30c3df47c8d"
};

const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
const auth = getAuth(app);
const provider = new GoogleAuthProvider();

const ADMIN_EMAILS = [
  "saybon.fr@gmail.com"
];

export async function adminLogin() {
  try {
    const result = await signInWithPopup(auth, provider);
    const user = result.user;

    if (!ADMIN_EMAILS.includes(user.email)) {
      alert("Access denied. Admin only.");
      await auth.signOut();
      return;
    }

    window.location.href = "/features/admin/";
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    alert("Admin login failed.");
  }
}

import { initializeApp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js";
import {
  getAuth,
  onAuthStateChanged
} from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-auth.js";

const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey: "AIzaSyB2aKUdE1NSt0kN332BwTYSX52D0lxj1g0",
  authDomain: "saybon-3e3c2.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId: "saybon-3e3c2",
  storageBucket: "saybon-3e3c2.appspot.com",
  messagingSenderId: "75085012344",
  appId: "1:75085012344:web:0b18581cb0a30c3df47c8d"
};

const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
const auth = getAuth(app);

const ADMIN_EMAILS = [
  "saybon.fr@gmail.com"
];

onAuthStateChanged(auth, (user) => {
  if (!user || !ADMIN_EMAILS.includes(user.email)) {
    alert("Admin access only.");
    window.location.href = "/index.html";
  }
});

}
pre{
  background:#f7f9fc;
  padding:18px;
  border-radius:12px;
  overflow:auto;
  white-space:pre-wrap;
  word-break:break-word;
}
.ok{color:green;font-weight:700}
.bad{color:red;font-weight:700}
</style>

<body>
<div class="card">
  <h1>SayBon DELF Debug Check</h1>
  <p>This page checks whether <strong>/features/delf/tests/prim.json</strong> is truly live.</p>
  <div id="status">Checking...</div>
  <pre id="output"></pre>
</div>

<script>
(async ()=>{
  const status = document.getElementById("status");
  const output = document.getElementById("output");

  try{
    const url = "/features/delf/tests/prim.json?ts=" + Date.now();
    const res = await fetch(url);
    const text = await res.text();

    status.innerHTML = '<span class="ok">SUCCESS: fetch worked</span>';
    output.textContent =
      "FETCH URL: " + url + "\n\n" +
      "HTTP STATUS: " + res.status + "\n\n" +
      "RAW RESPONSE:\n" + text;
  }catch(err){
    status.innerHTML = '<span class="bad">FAILED: fetch crashed</span>';
    output.textContent = err.message || String(err);
  }
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

(function(){
  const p = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

  const candidate = p.get("candidate") || "—";
  const level = p.get("level") || "A1";
  const score = parseInt(p.get("score") || "0");

  document.getElementById("candidate").textContent = candidate;

  let readiness = "A1 Readiness";
  let entry = "DELF Prim A1 Preparation";
  let text = "You are showing encouraging signs of readiness. With structured preparation, you will be fully ready for your exam.";

  if(score < 40){
    readiness = "Building Toward A1";
    entry = "DELF Prim A1 Preparation";
    text = "You are building the key skills needed for DELF Prim. With guided preparation, you will gain confidence and become fully ready.";
  }

  if(score >= 70){
    readiness = "Strong A1 / Moving Toward A2";
    entry = "DELF Prim A2 Preparation";
    text = "You are showing strong foundations and are ready to build toward a higher level with focused preparation.";
  }

  document.getElementById("readiness").textContent = readiness;
  document.getElementById("entry").textContent = entry;
  document.getElementById("title").textContent = entry;
  document.getElementById("text").textContent = text;
})();
</script>

<script type="module">

import { initializeApp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.2/firebase-app.js";
import { getFirestore, doc, setDoc } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.2/firebase-firestore.js";

const firebaseConfig = {
apiKey: "YOUR_API_KEY",
authDomain: "YOUR_DOMAIN",
projectId: "YOUR_PROJECT"
};

const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
const db = getFirestore(app);

function generateCode(){

const digits=Math.floor(1000+Math.random()*9000)
const letter=String.fromCharCode(65+Math.floor(Math.random()*26))

return `SB-DEL-${digits}${letter}`

}

window.createCandidate = async function(){

const name=document.getElementById("name").value
const ageGroup=document.getElementById("ageGroup").value

if(!name || !ageGroup){

alert("Please complete the form")
return

}

const code=generateCode()

await setDoc(doc(db,"candidates",code),{

name:name,
ageGroup:ageGroup,
createdAt:Date.now(),
recommendedLevel:null

})

document.getElementById("codeDisplay").innerHTML=

`Your Candidate Code: <br><b>${code}</b><br><br>
Save this code to return later.`

setTimeout(()=>{

if(ageGroup==="prim") location.href="tests/prim.html"
if(ageGroup==="junior") location.href="tests/junior.html"
if(ageGroup==="adult") location.href="tests/adult.html"

},3000)

}

</script>

<script>
const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey:"AIzaSyB2aKUdE1NSt0kN332BwTYSX52D0lxj1g0",
  authDomain:"saybon-3e3c2.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId:"saybon-3e3c2",
  storageBucket:"saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app",
  messagingSenderId:"75085012344",
  appId:"1:75085012344:web:0b18581cb0a30c3df47c8d"
};

firebase.initializeApp(firebaseConfig);

const db = firebase.firestore();
const storage = firebase.storage();

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const test = params.get("test") || "prim";

let testData = null;
let current = 0;
let answers = {};
let submitting = false;

let recorder = null;
let recorderStream = null;
let recorderChunks = [];
let recorderQuestionIndex = null;
let audioContext = null;
let analyser = null;
let sourceNode = null;
let waveAnimation = null;

function esc(str){
  return String(str ?? "")
    .replaceAll("&","&amp;")
    .replaceAll("<","&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">","&gt;")
    .replaceAll('"',"&quot;")
    .replaceAll("'","&#39;");
}

function typeLabel(type){
  if(type === "listening") return "Listening";
  if(type === "reading") return "Reading";
  if(type === "writing") return "Writing";
  if(type === "speaking") return "Speaking";
  return "Question";
}

function optionBadge(i){
  return ["A","B","C","D","E","F"][i] || String(i + 1);
}

function renderCurrentSlide(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  const stage = document.getElementById("stage");

  let html = `
    <section data-index="${current}">
      <div class="pill">${esc(typeLabel(q.type))}</div>
      <h2 class="questionText">${esc(q.question || "")}</h2>
  `;

  if(q.type === "listening"){
    html += `
      <div class="audioBox">
        <audio controls controlsList="nodownload" src="${esc(q.audio || "")}"></audio>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "reading" && q.text){
    html += `
      <div class="readingBox">${esc(q.text)}</div>
    `;
  }

  if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && Array.isArray(q.choices)){
    html += `<div class="answerGrid">`;
    q.choices.forEach((choice, i) => {
      const checked = String(answers[current] ?? "") === String(i) ? "checked" : "";
      html += `
        <label class="option">
          <input type="radio" name="q${current}" value="${i}" ${checked}>
          <span class="optionCard">
            <span class="badge">${optionBadge(i)}</span>
            <span>${esc(choice)}</span>
          </span>
        </label>
      `;
    });
    html += `</div>`;
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    html += `
      <div class="writingBox">
        ${q.prompt ? `<div class="readingBox" style="margin-bottom:14px;">${esc(q.prompt)}</div>` : ""}
        <textarea id="write${current}" placeholder="Type your answer here...">${esc(answers[current] || "")}</textarea>
        <div class="helper">Write clearly and answer only what is asked.</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "speaking"){
    const hasSaved = !!answers[current];
    const statusText = hasSaved ? "Recording saved." : "Press start, speak clearly, then stop.";
    html += `
      <div class="speakingBox">
        <div class="helper" style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:14px;">Your answer will be recorded and saved with your test.</div>
        <div class="recordControls">
          <button class="btn btnPrimary" type="button" id="startRecBtn" onclick="startRecording(${current})">Start recording</button>
          <button class="btn btnDanger" type="button" id="stopRecBtn" onclick="stopRecording()">Stop</button>
<button class="btn btnMuted" type="button" id="storageTestBtn" onclick="runStorageTest()">Test upload</button>
        </div>
        <div class="waveShell">
          <canvas id="waveCanvas" width="900" height="92"></canvas>
        </div>
        <div class="recStatus" id="recStatus">${esc(statusText)}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  html += `</section>`;
  stage.innerHTML = html;

  updateProgress();
  updateCenterNote();
}

function updateProgress(){
  const total = testData.questions.length;
  document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${current + 1} / ${total}`;
  document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = `${((current + 1) / total) * 100}%`;
  document.getElementById("backBtn").style.visibility = current === 0 ? "hidden" : "visible";
  document.getElementById("nextBtn").innerText = current === total - 1 ? "Finish" : "Next";
}

function updateCenterNote(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  let text = "Choose an answer, then continue.";
  if(q.type === "listening") text = "Listen carefully before choosing your answer.";
  if(q.type === "writing") text = "Take your time and write a complete answer.";
  if(q.type === "speaking") text = answers[current] ? "Recording captured. You can move on." : "Record your answer before moving on.";
  document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = text;
}

function saveCurrentAnswer(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];

  if(q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading"){
    const selected = document.querySelector(`input[name="q${current}"]:checked`);
    if(selected){
      answers[current] = selected.value;
    }
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    const box = document.getElementById(`write${current}`);
    if(box){
      answers[current] = box.value.trim();
    }
  }
}

function nextSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
    current += 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
    return;
  }

  submitTest();
}

function prevSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current > 0){
    current -= 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }
}

function drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx){
  if(!analyser) return;

  const bufferLength = analyser.fftSize;
  const dataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);

  function draw(){
    waveAnimation = requestAnimationFrame(draw);

    analyser.getByteTimeDomainData(dataArray);

    ctx.fillStyle = "#eef4ff";
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

    ctx.lineWidth = 2;
    ctx.strokeStyle = "#4f8cff";
    ctx.beginPath();

    const sliceWidth = canvas.width / bufferLength;
    let x = 0;

    for(let i=0;i<bufferLength;i++){
      const v = dataArray[i] / 128.0;
      const y = v * canvas.height / 2;

      if(i === 0){
        ctx.moveTo(x,y);
      }else{
        ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }

      x += sliceWidth;
    }

    ctx.lineTo(canvas.width, canvas.height / 2);
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  draw();
}

async function startRecording(index){
  try{
    if(recorder || recorderStream) return;

    recorderQuestionIndex = index;
    recorderChunks = [];

    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const canvas = document.getElementById("waveCanvas");
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");

    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = true;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = false;
    if(status) status.innerText = "Recording...";

    recorderStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio:true });

    audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(recorderStream);
    analyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
    analyser.fftSize = 2048;
    sourceNode.connect(analyser);

    drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx);

    recorder = new MediaRecorder(recorderStream);

    recorder.ondataavailable = (e)=>{
      if(e.data && e.data.size > 0){
        recorderChunks.push(e.data);
      }
    };

    recorder.onstop = async ()=>{
      let saveSucceeded = false;

      try{
        const blob = new Blob(recorderChunks, { type:"audio/webm" });
        const path = `placement-audio/${test}/${Date.now()}-${recorderQuestionIndex}.webm`;
        const ref = storage.ref(path);

        const uploadResult = await Promise.race([
          ref.put(blob),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("Upload timed out")), 20000);
          })
        ]);

        const url = await Promise.race([
          uploadResult.ref.getDownloadURL(),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("URL fetch timed out")), 10000);
          })
        ]);

        answers[recorderQuestionIndex] = url;
        saveSucceeded = true;

        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording saved.";
        updateCenterNote();
      }catch(err){
        const code = err?.code || "unknown-error";
        const message = err?.message || "No extra message";
        if(status) status.innerText = `Recording upload failed: ${code}`;
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR FULL:", err);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR CODE:", code);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR MESSAGE:", message);
        alert("UPLOAD ERROR:`n" + code + "`n`n" + message);
      }finally{
        if(recorderStream){
          recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
        }

        if(sourceNode){
          try{ sourceNode.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(analyser){
          try{ analyser.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(audioContext && audioContext.state !== "closed"){
          try{ await audioContext.close(); }catch(e){}
        }

        cancelAnimationFrame(waveAnimation);
        ctx.clearRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

        recorder = null;
        recorderStream = null;
        recorderChunks = [];
        recorderQuestionIndex = null;
        audioContext = null;
        analyser = null;
        sourceNode = null;
        waveAnimation = null;

        if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
        if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
      }

      if(saveSucceeded){
        setTimeout(()=>{
          if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
            current += 1;
            renderCurrentSlide();
          }else{
            submitTest();
          }
        }, 500);
      }
    };

    recorder.start();
  }catch(err){
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");

    if(status) status.innerText = "Microphone access failed.";
    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;

    console.error(err);
  }
}

function stopRecording(){
  if(!recorder) return;

  const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
  const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");

  if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
  if(status) status.innerText = "Saving recording...";

  if(recorderStream){
    recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
  }

  try{
    recorder.stop();
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    if(status) status.innerText = "Could not stop recording.";
  }
}

function scoreObjectiveAnswers(){
  let score = 0;

  testData.questions.forEach((q, index)=>{
    if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && typeof q.answer !== "undefined"){
      if(String(answers[index] ?? "") === String(q.answer)){
        score += 1;
      }
    }
  });

  return score;
}

async function submitTest(){
  if(submitting) return;
  submitting = true;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  const score = scoreObjectiveAnswers();

  try{
    await db.collection("placementTests").add({
      test,
      title: testData.title,
      answers,
      objectiveScore: score,
      totalQuestions: testData.questions.length,
      created: new Date()
    });

    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="finishBox">
        <h2>Test submitted</h2>
        <p>Your responses have been saved successfully.</p>
        <button class="btn btnPrimary" onclick="window.location='/dashboard/index.html'">Return to dashboard</button>
      </div>
    `;

    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "Submission complete.";
    document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = "100%";
    document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${testData.questions.length} / ${testData.questions.length}`;
  }catch(err){
    submitting = false;
    alert("Submission failed. Please try again.");
    console.error(err);
  }
}

async function loadTest(){
  try{
    const res = await fetch(`/features/delf/tests/${test}.json`);
    if(!res.ok){
      throw new Error("Test file not found");
    }

    testData = await res.json();

    document.getElementById("title").innerText = testData.title || "Placement Test";
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }catch(err){
    document.getElementById("title").innerText = "Test unavailable";
    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="errorBox">
        <h2>We couldn't load this test.</h2>
        <p>Please check the test link or try again later.</p>
      </div>
    `;
    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "No test loaded.";
    console.error(err);
  }
}


async function runStorageTest(){
  try{
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    if(status) status.innerText = "Running storage test...";

    console.log("=== STORAGE SELF TEST START ===");
    console.log("Firebase app:", firebase.app().options);
    console.log("Storage bucket from config:", firebase.app().options.storageBucket);

    const blob = new Blob(["SayBon storage test"], { type: "text/plain" });
    const path = `debug/test-${Date.now()}.txt`;
    const ref = storage.ref(path);

    console.log("Storage ref fullPath:", ref.fullPath);
    console.log("Uploading tiny test file...");

    const snap = await ref.put(blob);
    console.log("Upload snapshot:", snap);

    const url = await ref.getDownloadURL();
    console.log("STORAGE TEST SUCCESS URL:", url);

    if(status) status.innerText = "Storage test passed.";
    alert("STORAGE TEST PASSED`n`nFile uploaded successfully.");
  }catch(err){
    const code = err?.code || "unknown-error";
    const message = err?.message || "No extra message";

    console.error("=== STORAGE SELF TEST FAILED ===");
    console.error("STORAGE TEST FULL ERROR:", err);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST CODE:", code);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST MESSAGE:", message);

    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    if(status) status.innerText = `Storage test failed: ${code}`;

    alert("STORAGE TEST FAILED`n`n" + code + "`n`n" + message);
  }
}

loadTest();
</script>

<script>
const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey:"AIzaSyB2aKUdE1NSt0kN332BwTYSX52D0lxj1g0",
  authDomain:"saybon-3e3c2.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId:"saybon-3e3c2",
  storageBucket:"saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app",
  messagingSenderId:"75085012344",
  appId:"1:75085012344:web:0b18581cb0a30c3df47c8d"
};

firebase.initializeApp(firebaseConfig);

const db = firebase.firestore();
const storage = firebase.storage();

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const test = params.get("test") || "prim";

let testData = null;
let current = 0;
let answers = {};
let submitting = false;

let recorder = null;
let recorderStream = null;
let recorderChunks = [];
let recorderQuestionIndex = null;
let audioContext = null;
let analyser = null;
let sourceNode = null;
let waveAnimation = null;

function esc(str){
  return String(str ?? "")
    .replaceAll("&","&amp;")
    .replaceAll("<","&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">","&gt;")
    .replaceAll('"',"&quot;")
    .replaceAll("'","&#39;");
}

function typeLabel(type){
  if(type === "listening") return "Listening";
  if(type === "reading") return "Reading";
  if(type === "writing") return "Writing";
  if(type === "speaking") return "Speaking";
  return "Question";
}

function optionBadge(i){
  return ["A","B","C","D","E","F"][i] || String(i + 1);
}

function renderCurrentSlide(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  const stage = document.getElementById("stage");

  let html = `
    <section data-index="${current}">
      <div class="pill">${esc(typeLabel(q.type))}</div>
      <h2 class="questionText">${esc(q.question || "")}</h2>
  `;

  if(q.type === "listening"){
    html += `
      <div class="audioBox">
        <audio controls controlsList="nodownload" src="${esc(q.audio || "")}"></audio>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "reading" && q.text){
    html += `
      <div class="readingBox">${esc(q.text)}</div>
    `;
  }

  if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && Array.isArray(q.choices)){
    html += `<div class="answerGrid">`;
    q.choices.forEach((choice, i) => {
      const checked = String(answers[current] ?? "") === String(i) ? "checked" : "";
      html += `
        <label class="option">
          <input type="radio" name="q${current}" value="${i}" ${checked}>
          <span class="optionCard">
            <span class="badge">${optionBadge(i)}</span>
            <span>${esc(choice)}</span>
          </span>
        </label>
      `;
    });
    html += `</div>`;
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    html += `
      <div class="writingBox">
        ${q.prompt ? `<div class="readingBox" style="margin-bottom:14px;">${esc(q.prompt)}</div>` : ""}
        <textarea id="write${current}" placeholder="Type your answer here...">${esc(answers[current] || "")}</textarea>
        <div class="helper">Write clearly and answer only what is asked.</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "speaking"){
    const hasSaved = !!answers[current];
    const statusText = hasSaved ? "Recording saved." : "Press start, speak clearly, then stop.";
    html += `
      <div class="speakingBox">
        <div class="helper" style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:14px;">Your answer will be recorded and saved with your test.</div>
        <div class="recordControls">
          <button class="btn btnPrimary" type="button" id="startRecBtn" onclick="startRecording(${current})">Start recording</button>
          <button class="btn btnDanger" type="button" id="stopRecBtn" onclick="stopRecording()">Stop</button>
        </div>
        <div class="waveShell">
          <canvas id="waveCanvas" width="900" height="92"></canvas>
        </div>
        <div class="recStatus" id="recStatus">${esc(statusText)}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  html += `</section>`;
  stage.innerHTML = html;

  updateProgress();
  updateCenterNote();
}

function updateProgress(){
  const total = testData.questions.length;
  document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${current + 1} / ${total}`;
  document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = `${((current + 1) / total) * 100}%`;
  document.getElementById("backBtn").style.visibility = current === 0 ? "hidden" : "visible";
  document.getElementById("nextBtn").innerText = current === total - 1 ? "Finish" : "Next";
}

function updateCenterNote(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  let text = "Choose an answer, then continue.";
  if(q.type === "listening") text = "Listen carefully before choosing your answer.";
  if(q.type === "writing") text = "Take your time and write a complete answer.";
  if(q.type === "speaking") text = answers[current] ? "Recording captured. You can move on." : "Record your answer before moving on.";
  document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = text;
}

function saveCurrentAnswer(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];

  if(q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading"){
    const selected = document.querySelector(`input[name="q${current}"]:checked`);
    if(selected){
      answers[current] = selected.value;
    }
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    const box = document.getElementById(`write${current}`);
    if(box){
      answers[current] = box.value.trim();
    }
  }
}

function nextSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
    current += 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
    return;
  }

  submitTest();
}

function prevSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current > 0){
    current -= 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }
}

function drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx){
  if(!analyser) return;

  const bufferLength = analyser.fftSize;
  const dataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);

  function draw(){
    waveAnimation = requestAnimationFrame(draw);

    analyser.getByteTimeDomainData(dataArray);

    ctx.fillStyle = "#eef4ff";
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

    ctx.lineWidth = 2;
    ctx.strokeStyle = "#4f8cff";
    ctx.beginPath();

    const sliceWidth = canvas.width / bufferLength;
    let x = 0;

    for(let i=0;i<bufferLength;i++){
      const v = dataArray[i] / 128.0;
      const y = v * canvas.height / 2;

      if(i === 0){
        ctx.moveTo(x,y);
      }else{
        ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }

      x += sliceWidth;
    }

    ctx.lineTo(canvas.width, canvas.height / 2);
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  draw();
}

async function startRecording(index){
  try{
    if(recorder || recorderStream) return;

    recorderQuestionIndex = index;
    recorderChunks = [];

    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const canvas = document.getElementById("waveCanvas");
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");

    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = true;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = false;
    if(status) status.innerText = "Recording...";

    recorderStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio:true });

    audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(recorderStream);
    analyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
    analyser.fftSize = 2048;
    sourceNode.connect(analyser);

    drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx);

    recorder = new MediaRecorder(recorderStream);

    recorder.ondataavailable = (e)=>{
      if(e.data && e.data.size > 0){
        recorderChunks.push(e.data);
      }
    };

    recorder.onstop = async ()=>{
      let saveSucceeded = false;

      try{
        const blob = new Blob(recorderChunks, { type:"audio/webm" });
        const path = `placement-audio/${test}/${Date.now()}-${recorderQuestionIndex}.webm`;
        const ref = storage.ref(path);

        const uploadResult = await Promise.race([
          ref.put(blob),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("Upload timed out")), 20000);
          })
        ]);

        const url = await Promise.race([
          uploadResult.ref.getDownloadURL(),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("URL fetch timed out")), 10000);
          })
        ]);

        answers[recorderQuestionIndex] = url;
        saveSucceeded = true;

        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording saved.";
        updateCenterNote();
      }catch(err){
        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording upload failed.";
        console.error(err);
      }finally{
        if(recorderStream){
          recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
        }

        if(sourceNode){
          try{ sourceNode.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(analyser){
          try{ analyser.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(audioContext && audioContext.state !== "closed"){
          try{ await audioContext.close(); }catch(e){}
        }

        cancelAnimationFrame(waveAnimation);
        ctx.clearRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

        recorder = null;
        recorderStream = null;
        recorderChunks = [];
        recorderQuestionIndex = null;
        audioContext = null;
        analyser = null;
        sourceNode = null;
        waveAnimation = null;

        if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
        if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
      }

      if(saveSucceeded){
        setTimeout(()=>{
          if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
            current += 1;
            renderCurrentSlide();
          }else{
            submitTest();
          }
        }, 500);
      }
    };

    recorder.start();
  }catch(err){
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");

    if(status) status.innerText = "Microphone access failed.";
    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;

    console.error(err);
  }
}

function stopRecording(){
  if(!recorder) return;

  const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
  const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");

  if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
  if(status) status.innerText = "Saving recording...";

  if(recorderStream){
    recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
  }

  try{
    recorder.stop();
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    if(status) status.innerText = "Could not stop recording.";
  }
}

function scoreObjectiveAnswers(){
  let score = 0;

  testData.questions.forEach((q, index)=>{
    if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && typeof q.answer !== "undefined"){
      if(String(answers[index] ?? "") === String(q.answer)){
        score += 1;
      }
    }
  });

  return score;
}

async function submitTest(){
  if(submitting) return;
  submitting = true;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  const score = scoreObjectiveAnswers();

  try{
    await db.collection("placementTests").add({
      test,
      title: testData.title,
      answers,
      objectiveScore: score,
      totalQuestions: testData.questions.length,
      created: new Date()
    });

    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="finishBox">
        <h2>Test submitted</h2>
        <p>Your responses have been saved successfully.</p>
        <button class="btn btnPrimary" onclick="window.location='/dashboard/index.html'">Return to dashboard</button>
      </div>
    `;

    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "Submission complete.";
    document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = "100%";
    document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${testData.questions.length} / ${testData.questions.length}`;
  }catch(err){
    submitting = false;
    alert("Submission failed. Please try again.");
    console.error(err);
  }
}

async function loadTest(){
  try{
    const res = await fetch(`/features/delf/tests/${test}.json`);
    if(!res.ok){
      throw new Error("Test file not found");
    }

    testData = await res.json();

    document.getElementById("title").innerText = testData.title || "Placement Test";
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }catch(err){
    document.getElementById("title").innerText = "Test unavailable";
    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="errorBox">
        <h2>We couldn't load this test.</h2>
        <p>Please check the test link or try again later.</p>
      </div>
    `;
    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "No test loaded.";
    console.error(err);
  }
}

loadTest();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey:"AIzaSyB2aKUdE1NSt0kN332BwTYSX52D0lxj1g0",
  authDomain:"saybon-3e3c2.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId:"saybon-3e3c2",
  storageBucket:"saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app",
  messagingSenderId:"75085012344",
  appId:"1:75085012344:web:0b18581cb0a30c3df47c8d"
};

firebase.initializeApp(firebaseConfig);

const db = firebase.firestore();
const storage = firebase.app().storage("gs://saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app");

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const test = params.get("test") || "prim";

let testData = null;
let current = 0;
let answers = {};
let submitting = false;

let recorder = null;
let recorderStream = null;
let recorderChunks = [];
let recorderQuestionIndex = null;
let audioContext = null;
let analyser = null;
let sourceNode = null;
let waveAnimation = null;

function esc(str){
  return String(str ?? "")
    .replaceAll("&","&amp;")
    .replaceAll("<","&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">","&gt;")
    .replaceAll('"',"&quot;")
    .replaceAll("'","&#39;");
}

function typeLabel(type){
  if(type === "listening") return "Listening";
  if(type === "reading") return "Reading";
  if(type === "writing") return "Writing";
  if(type === "speaking") return "Speaking";
  return "Question";
}

function optionBadge(i){
  return ["A","B","C","D","E","F"][i] || String(i + 1);
}

function renderCurrentSlide(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  const stage = document.getElementById("stage");

  let html = `
    <section data-index="${current}">
      <div class="pill">${esc(typeLabel(q.type))}</div>
      <h2 class="questionText">${esc(q.question || "")}</h2>
  `;

  if(q.type === "listening"){
    html += `
      <div class="audioBox">
        <audio controls controlsList="nodownload" src="${esc(q.audio || "")}"></audio>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "reading" && q.text){
    html += `
      <div class="readingBox">${esc(q.text)}</div>
    `;
  }

  if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && Array.isArray(q.choices)){
    html += `<div class="answerGrid">`;
    q.choices.forEach((choice, i) => {
      const checked = String(answers[current] ?? "") === String(i) ? "checked" : "";
      html += `
        <label class="option">
          <input type="radio" name="q${current}" value="${i}" ${checked}>
          <span class="optionCard">
            <span class="badge">${optionBadge(i)}</span>
            <span>${esc(choice)}</span>
          </span>
        </label>
      `;
    });
    html += `</div>`;
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    html += `
      <div class="writingBox">
        ${q.prompt ? `<div class="readingBox" style="margin-bottom:14px;">${esc(q.prompt)}</div>` : ""}
        <textarea id="write${current}" placeholder="Type your answer here...">${esc(answers[current] || "")}</textarea>
        <div class="helper">Write clearly and answer only what is asked.</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "speaking"){
    const hasSaved = !!answers[current];
    const statusText = hasSaved ? "Recording saved." : "Press start, speak clearly, then stop.";
    html += `
      <div class="speakingBox">
        <div class="helper" style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:14px;">Your answer will be recorded and saved with your test.</div>
        <div class="recordControls">
          <button class="btn btnPrimary" type="button" id="startRecBtn" onclick="startRecording(${current})">Start recording</button>
          <button class="btn btnDanger" type="button" id="stopRecBtn" onclick="stopRecording()">Stop</button>
<button class="btn btnMuted" type="button" id="storageTestBtn" onclick="runStorageTest()">Test upload</button>
        </div>
        <div class="waveShell">
          <canvas id="waveCanvas" width="900" height="92"></canvas>
        </div>
        <div class="recStatus" id="recStatus">${esc(statusText)}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  html += `</section>`;
  stage.innerHTML = html;

  updateProgress();
  updateCenterNote();
}

function updateProgress(){
  const total = testData.questions.length;
  document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${current + 1} / ${total}`;
  document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = `${((current + 1) / total) * 100}%`;
  document.getElementById("backBtn").style.visibility = current === 0 ? "hidden" : "visible";
  document.getElementById("nextBtn").innerText = current === total - 1 ? "Finish" : "Next";
}

function updateCenterNote(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  let text = "Choose an answer, then continue.";
  if(q.type === "listening") text = "Listen carefully before choosing your answer.";
  if(q.type === "writing") text = "Take your time and write a complete answer.";
  if(q.type === "speaking") text = answers[current] ? "Recording captured. You can move on." : "Record your answer before moving on.";
  document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = text;
}

function saveCurrentAnswer(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];

  if(q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading"){
    const selected = document.querySelector(`input[name="q${current}"]:checked`);
    if(selected){
      answers[current] = selected.value;
    }
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    const box = document.getElementById(`write${current}`);
    if(box){
      answers[current] = box.value.trim();
    }
  }
}

function nextSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
    current += 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
    return;
  }

  submitTest();
}

function prevSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current > 0){
    current -= 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }
}

function drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx){
  if(!analyser) return;

  const bufferLength = analyser.fftSize;
  const dataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);

  function draw(){
    waveAnimation = requestAnimationFrame(draw);

    analyser.getByteTimeDomainData(dataArray);

    ctx.fillStyle = "#eef4ff";
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

    ctx.lineWidth = 2;
    ctx.strokeStyle = "#4f8cff";
    ctx.beginPath();

    const sliceWidth = canvas.width / bufferLength;
    let x = 0;

    for(let i=0;i<bufferLength;i++){
      const v = dataArray[i] / 128.0;
      const y = v * canvas.height / 2;

      if(i === 0){
        ctx.moveTo(x,y);
      }else{
        ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }

      x += sliceWidth;
    }

    ctx.lineTo(canvas.width, canvas.height / 2);
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  draw();
}

async function startRecording(index){
  try{
    if(recorder || recorderStream) return;

    recorderQuestionIndex = index;
    recorderChunks = [];

    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const canvas = document.getElementById("waveCanvas");
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");

    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = true;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = false;
    if(status) status.innerText = "Recording...";

    recorderStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio:true });

    audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(recorderStream);
    analyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
    analyser.fftSize = 2048;
    sourceNode.connect(analyser);

    drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx);

    recorder = new MediaRecorder(recorderStream);

    recorder.ondataavailable = (e)=>{
      if(e.data && e.data.size > 0){
        recorderChunks.push(e.data);
      }
    };

    recorder.onstop = async ()=>{
      let saveSucceeded = false;

      try{
        const blob = new Blob(recorderChunks, { type:"audio/webm" });
        const path = `placement-audio/${test}/${Date.now()}-${recorderQuestionIndex}.webm`;
        const ref = storage.ref(path);

        const uploadResult = await Promise.race([
          ref.put(blob),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("Upload timed out")), 20000);
          })
        ]);

        const url = await Promise.race([
          uploadResult.ref.getDownloadURL(),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("URL fetch timed out")), 10000);
          })
        ]);

        answers[recorderQuestionIndex] = url;
        saveSucceeded = true;

        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording saved.";
        updateCenterNote();
      }catch(err){
        const code = err?.code || "unknown-error";
        const message = err?.message || "No extra message";
        const serverResponse = err?.serverResponse || "No serverResponse";
        const customData = JSON.stringify(err?.customData || {}, null, 2);

        if(status) status.innerText = `Recording upload failed: ${code}`;

        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR FULL:", err);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR CODE:", code);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR MESSAGE:", message);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR SERVER RESPONSE:", serverResponse);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR CUSTOM DATA:", customData);

        alert(
          "UPLOAD ERROR:`n" + code +
          "`n`nMESSAGE:`n" + message +
          "`n`nSERVER RESPONSE:`n" + serverResponse +
          "`n`nCUSTOM DATA:`n" + customData
        );
      }finally{
        if(recorderStream){
          recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
        }

        if(sourceNode){
          try{ sourceNode.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(analyser){
          try{ analyser.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(audioContext && audioContext.state !== "closed"){
          try{ await audioContext.close(); }catch(e){}
        }

        cancelAnimationFrame(waveAnimation);
        ctx.clearRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

        recorder = null;
        recorderStream = null;
        recorderChunks = [];
        recorderQuestionIndex = null;
        audioContext = null;
        analyser = null;
        sourceNode = null;
        waveAnimation = null;

        if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
        if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
      }

      if(saveSucceeded){
        setTimeout(()=>{
          if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
            current += 1;
            renderCurrentSlide();
          }else{
            submitTest();
          }
        }, 500);
      }
    };

    recorder.start();
  }catch(err){
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");

    if(status) status.innerText = "Microphone access failed.";
    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;

    console.error(err);
  }
}

function stopRecording(){
  if(!recorder) return;

  const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
  const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");

  if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
  if(status) status.innerText = "Saving recording...";

  if(recorderStream){
    recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
  }

  try{
    recorder.stop();
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    if(status) status.innerText = "Could not stop recording.";
  }
}

function scoreObjectiveAnswers(){
  let score = 0;

  testData.questions.forEach((q, index)=>{
    if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && typeof q.answer !== "undefined"){
      if(String(answers[index] ?? "") === String(q.answer)){
        score += 1;
      }
    }
  });

  return score;
}

async function submitTest(){
  if(submitting) return;
  submitting = true;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  const score = scoreObjectiveAnswers();

  try{
    await db.collection("placementTests").add({
      test,
      title: testData.title,
      answers,
      objectiveScore: score,
      totalQuestions: testData.questions.length,
      created: new Date()
    });

    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="finishBox">
        <h2>Test submitted</h2>
        <p>Your responses have been saved successfully.</p>
        <button class="btn btnPrimary" onclick="window.location='/dashboard/index.html'">Return to dashboard</button>
      </div>
    `;

    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "Submission complete.";
    document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = "100%";
    document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${testData.questions.length} / ${testData.questions.length}`;
  }catch(err){
    submitting = false;
    alert("Submission failed. Please try again.");
    console.error(err);
  }
}

async function loadTest(){
  try{
    const res = await fetch(`/features/delf/tests/${test}.json`);
    if(!res.ok){
      throw new Error("Test file not found");
    }

    testData = await res.json();

    document.getElementById("title").innerText = testData.title || "Placement Test";
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }catch(err){
    document.getElementById("title").innerText = "Test unavailable";
    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="errorBox">
        <h2>We couldn't load this test.</h2>
        <p>Please check the test link or try again later.</p>
      </div>
    `;
    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "No test loaded.";
    console.error(err);
  }
}


async function runStorageTest(){
  try{
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    if(status) status.innerText = "Running storage test...";

    console.log("=== STORAGE SELF TEST START ===");
    console.log("Firebase app:", firebase.app().options);
    console.log("Storage bucket from config:", firebase.app().options.storageBucket);

    const blob = new Blob(["SayBon storage test"], { type: "text/plain" });
    const path = `debug/test-${Date.now()}.txt`;
    const ref = storage.ref(path);

    console.log("Storage ref fullPath:", ref.fullPath);
    console.log("Uploading tiny test file...");

    const snap = await ref.put(blob);
    console.log("Upload snapshot:", snap);

    const url = await ref.getDownloadURL();
    console.log("STORAGE TEST SUCCESS URL:", url);

    if(status) status.innerText = "Storage test passed.";
    alert("STORAGE TEST PASSED`n`nFile uploaded successfully.");
  }catch(err){
    const code = err?.code || "unknown-error";
    const message = err?.message || "No extra message";
    const serverResponse = err?.serverResponse || "No serverResponse";
    const customData = JSON.stringify(err?.customData || {}, null, 2);

    console.error("=== STORAGE SELF TEST FAILED ===");
    console.error("STORAGE TEST FULL ERROR:", err);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST CODE:", code);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST MESSAGE:", message);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST SERVER RESPONSE:", serverResponse);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST CUSTOM DATA:", customData);

    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    if(status) status.innerText = `Storage test failed: ${code}`;

    alert(
      "STORAGE TEST FAILED`n`n" + code +
      "`n`nMESSAGE:`n" + message +
      "`n`nSERVER RESPONSE:`n" + serverResponse +
      "`n`nCUSTOM DATA:`n" + customData
    );
  }
}

    </div>
