<script>
const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey:"AIzaSyB2aKUdE1NSt0kN332BwTYSX52D0lxj1g0",
  authDomain:"saybon-3e3c2.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId:"saybon-3e3c2",
  storageBucket:"saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app",
  messagingSenderId:"75085012344",
  appId:"1:75085012344:web:0b18581cb0a30c3df47c8d"
};

firebase.initializeApp(firebaseConfig);

const db = firebase.firestore();
const storage = firebase.app().storage("gs://saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app");

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const test = params.get("test") || "prim";

let testData = null;
let current = 0;
let answers = {};
let submitting = false;

let recorder = null;
let recorderStream = null;
let recorderChunks = [];
let recorderQuestionIndex = null;
let audioContext = null;
let analyser = null;
let sourceNode = null;
let waveAnimation = null;

function esc(str){
  return String(str ?? "")
    .replaceAll("&","&amp;")
    .replaceAll("<","&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">","&gt;")
    .replaceAll('"',"&quot;")
    .replaceAll("'","&#39;");
}

function typeLabel(type){
  if(type === "listening") return "Listening";
  if(type === "reading") return "Reading";
  if(type === "writing") return "Writing";
  if(type === "speaking") return "Speaking";
  return "Question";
}

function optionBadge(i){
  return ["A","B","C","D","E","F"][i] || String(i + 1);
}

function renderCurrentSlide(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  const stage = document.getElementById("stage");

  let html = `
    <section data-index="${current}">
      <div class="pill">${esc(typeLabel(q.type))}</div>
      <h2 class="questionText">${esc(q.question || "")}</h2>
  `;

  if(q.type === "listening"){
    html += `
      <div class="audioBox">
        <audio controls controlsList="nodownload" src="${esc(q.audio || "")}"></audio>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "reading" && q.text){
    html += `
      <div class="readingBox">${esc(q.text)}</div>
    `;
  }

  if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && Array.isArray(q.choices)){
    html += `<div class="answerGrid">`;
    q.choices.forEach((choice, i) => {
      const checked = String(answers[current] ?? "") === String(i) ? "checked" : "";
      html += `
        <label class="option">
          <input type="radio" name="q${current}" value="${i}" ${checked}>
          <span class="optionCard">
            <span class="badge">${optionBadge(i)}</span>
            <span>${esc(choice)}</span>
          </span>
        </label>
      `;
    });
    html += `</div>`;
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    html += `
      <div class="writingBox">
        ${q.prompt ? `<div class="readingBox" style="margin-bottom:14px;">${esc(q.prompt)}</div>` : ""}
        <textarea id="write${current}" placeholder="Type your answer here...">${esc(answers[current] || "")}</textarea>
        <div class="helper">Write clearly and answer only what is asked.</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "speaking"){
    const hasSaved = !!answers[current];
    const statusText = hasSaved ? "Recording saved." : "Press start, speak clearly, then stop.";
    html += `
      <div class="speakingBox">
        <div class="helper" style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:14px;">Your answer will be recorded and saved with your test.</div>
        <div class="recordControls">
          <button class="btn btnPrimary" type="button" id="startRecBtn" onclick="startRecording(${current})">Start recording</button>
          <button class="btn btnDanger" type="button" id="stopRecBtn" onclick="stopRecording()">Stop</button>
<button class="btn btnMuted" type="button" id="storageTestBtn" onclick="runStorageTest()">Test upload</button>
        </div>
        <div class="waveShell">
          <canvas id="waveCanvas" width="900" height="92"></canvas>
        </div>
        <div class="recStatus" id="recStatus">${esc(statusText)}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  html += `</section>`;
  stage.innerHTML = html;

  updateProgress();
  updateCenterNote();
}

function updateProgress(){
  const total = testData.questions.length;
  document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${current + 1} / ${total}`;
  document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = `${((current + 1) / total) * 100}%`;
  document.getElementById("backBtn").style.visibility = current === 0 ? "hidden" : "visible";
  document.getElementById("nextBtn").innerText = current === total - 1 ? "Finish" : "Next";
}

function updateCenterNote(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  let text = "Choose an answer, then continue.";
  if(q.type === "listening") text = "Listen carefully before choosing your answer.";
  if(q.type === "writing") text = "Take your time and write a complete answer.";
  if(q.type === "speaking") text = answers[current] ? "Recording captured. You can move on." : "Record your answer before moving on.";
  document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = text;
}

function saveCurrentAnswer(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];

  if(q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading"){
    const selected = document.querySelector(`input[name="q${current}"]:checked`);
    if(selected){
      answers[current] = selected.value;
    }
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    const box = document.getElementById(`write${current}`);
    if(box){
      answers[current] = box.value.trim();
    }
  }
}

function nextSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
    current += 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
    return;
  }

  submitTest();
}

function prevSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current > 0){
    current -= 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }
}

function drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx){
  if(!analyser) return;

  const bufferLength = analyser.fftSize;
  const dataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);

  function draw(){
    waveAnimation = requestAnimationFrame(draw);

    analyser.getByteTimeDomainData(dataArray);

    ctx.fillStyle = "#eef4ff";
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

    ctx.lineWidth = 2;
    ctx.strokeStyle = "#4f8cff";
    ctx.beginPath();

    const sliceWidth = canvas.width / bufferLength;
    let x = 0;

    for(let i=0;i<bufferLength;i++){
      const v = dataArray[i] / 128.0;
      const y = v * canvas.height / 2;

      if(i === 0){
        ctx.moveTo(x,y);
      }else{
        ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }

      x += sliceWidth;
    }

    ctx.lineTo(canvas.width, canvas.height / 2);
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  draw();
}

async function startRecording(index){
  try{
    if(recorder || recorderStream) return;

    recorderQuestionIndex = index;
    recorderChunks = [];

    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const canvas = document.getElementById("waveCanvas");
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");

    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = true;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = false;
    if(status) status.innerText = "Recording...";

    recorderStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio:true });

    audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(recorderStream);
    analyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
    analyser.fftSize = 2048;
    sourceNode.connect(analyser);

    drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx);

    recorder = new MediaRecorder(recorderStream);

    recorder.ondataavailable = (e)=>{
      if(e.data && e.data.size > 0){
        recorderChunks.push(e.data);
      }
    };

    recorder.onstop = async ()=>{
      let saveSucceeded = false;

      try{
        const blob = new Blob(recorderChunks, { type:"audio/webm" });
        const path = `placement-audio/${test}/${Date.now()}-${recorderQuestionIndex}.webm`;
        const ref = storage.ref(path);
        dumpStorageInfo("RECORDER BEFORE PUT", ref);
        dumpStorageContext("RECORDER PUT", ref);

        const uploadResult = await Promise.race([
          ref.put(blob),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("Upload timed out")), 20000);
          })
        ]);

        const url = await Promise.race([
          uploadResult.ref.getDownloadURL(),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("URL fetch timed out")), 10000);
          })
        ]);

        answers[recorderQuestionIndex] = url;
        saveSucceeded = true;

        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording saved.";
        updateCenterNote();
      }catch(err){
        const code = err?.code || "unknown-error";
        const message = err?.message || "No extra message";
        const serverResponse = err?.serverResponse || "No serverResponse";
        const customData = JSON.stringify(err?.customData || {}, null, 2);

        if(status) status.innerText = `Recording upload failed: ${code}`;

        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR FULL:", err);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR CODE:", code);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR MESSAGE:", message);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR SERVER RESPONSE:", serverResponse);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR CUSTOM DATA:", customData);

        alert(
          "UPLOAD ERROR:`n" + code +
          "`n`nMESSAGE:`n" + message +
          "`n`nSERVER RESPONSE:`n" + serverResponse +
          "`n`nCUSTOM DATA:`n" + customData
        );
      }finally{
        if(recorderStream){
          recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
        }

        if(sourceNode){
          try{ sourceNode.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(analyser){
          try{ analyser.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(audioContext && audioContext.state !== "closed"){
          try{ await audioContext.close(); }catch(e){}
        }

        cancelAnimationFrame(waveAnimation);
        ctx.clearRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

        recorder = null;
        recorderStream = null;
        recorderChunks = [];
        recorderQuestionIndex = null;
        audioContext = null;
        analyser = null;
        sourceNode = null;
        waveAnimation = null;

        if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
        if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
      }

      if(saveSucceeded){
        setTimeout(()=>{
          if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
            current += 1;
            renderCurrentSlide();
          }else{
            submitTest();
          }
        }, 500);
      }
    };

    recorder.start();
  }catch(err){
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");

    if(status) status.innerText = "Microphone access failed.";
    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;

    console.error(err);
  }
}

function stopRecording(){
  if(!recorder) return;

  const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
  const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");

  if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
  if(status) status.innerText = "Saving recording...";

  if(recorderStream){
    recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
  }

  try{
    recorder.stop();
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    if(status) status.innerText = "Could not stop recording.";
  }
}

function scoreObjectiveAnswers(){
  let score = 0;

  testData.questions.forEach((q, index)=>{
    if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && typeof q.answer !== "undefined"){
      if(String(answers[index] ?? "") === String(q.answer)){
        score += 1;
      }
    }
  });

  return score;
}

async function submitTest(){
  if(submitting) return;
  submitting = true;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  const score = scoreObjectiveAnswers();

  try{
    await db.collection("placementTests").add({
      test,
      title: testData.title,
      answers,
      objectiveScore: score,
      totalQuestions: testData.questions.length,
      created: new Date()
    });

    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="finishBox">
        <h2>Test submitted</h2>
        <p>Your responses have been saved successfully.</p>
        <button class="btn btnPrimary" onclick="window.location='/dashboard/index.html'">Return to dashboard</button>
      </div>
    `;

    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "Submission complete.";
    document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = "100%";
    document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${testData.questions.length} / ${testData.questions.length}`;
  }catch(err){
    submitting = false;
    alert("Submission failed. Please try again.");
    console.error(err);
  }
}

async function loadTest(){
  try{
    const res = await fetch(`/features/delf/tests/${test}.json`);
    if(!res.ok){
      throw new Error("Test file not found");
    }

    testData = await res.json();

    document.getElementById("title").innerText = testData.title || "Placement Test";
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }catch(err){
    document.getElementById("title").innerText = "Test unavailable";
    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="errorBox">
        <h2>We couldn't load this test.</h2>
        <p>Please check the test link or try again later.</p>
      </div>
    `;
    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "No test loaded.";
    console.error(err);
  }
}

  try{
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    if(status) status.innerText = "Running storage test...";

    console.log("=== STORAGE SELF TEST START ===");

        dumpStorageInfo("RECORDER BEFORE PUT", ref);
        dumpStorageContext("RECORDER PUT", ref);

    console.log("Storage ref fullPath:", ref.fullPath);
    console.log("Uploading tiny test file...");

    const url = await ref.getDownloadURL();

    console.error("STORAGE TEST MESSAGE:", message);

      "STORAGE TEST FAILED`n`n" + code +

      "`n`nCUSTOM DATA:`n" + customData
    );
  }
}


function showDebug(msg){
  const panel = document.getElementById("debugPanel");
  if(!panel) return;
  panel.style.display = "block";
  panel.textContent += "\n" + msg;
}

function clearDebug(){
  const panel = document.getElementById("debugPanel");
  if(!panel) return;
  panel.style.display = "block";
  panel.textContent = "=== SAYBON STORAGE FORENSIC LOG ===\n";
}

function dumpStorageContext(label, refObj){
  try{
    showDebug("[" + label + "]");
    showDebug("location.href = " + window.location.href);
    showDebug("origin = " + window.location.origin);
    showDebug("firebase app projectId = " + firebase.app().options.projectId);
    showDebug("firebase app storageBucket = " + firebase.app().options.storageBucket);
    showDebug("storage bucket via SDK = " + storage.app.options.storageBucket);
    if(refObj){
      showDebug("ref.fullPath = " + (refObj.fullPath || "n/a"));
      showDebug("ref.bucket = " + (refObj.bucket || "n/a"));
      showDebug("ref.name = " + (refObj.name || "n/a"));
      showDebug("ref.toString() = " + (refObj.toString ? refObj.toString() : "n/a"));
    }
    showDebug("----------------------------------------");
  }catch(err){
    console.error("dumpStorageContext error", err);
  }
}

async function runStorageForensics(){
  clearDebug();

  try{
    showDebug("Starting storage forensic test...");

    const testBlob = new Blob(["SayBon forensic test"], { type: "text/plain" });
    const testPath = "forensic-tests/" + Date.now() + "-forensic.txt";
    const ref = storage.ref(testPath);

    dumpStorageContext("BEFORE PUT", ref);

    await ref.put(testBlob);

    showDebug("PUT SUCCESS");

    const url = await ref.getDownloadURL();
    showDebug("DOWNLOAD URL SUCCESS");
    showDebug("downloadURL = " + url);

    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    if(status) status.innerText = "Storage forensic test passed.";
    alert("STORAGE FORENSIC TEST PASSED");
  }catch(err){
    const code = err?.code || "unknown-error";
    const message = err?.message || "No extra message";
    const serverResponse = err?.serverResponse || "No serverResponse";
    const customData = JSON.stringify(err?.customData || {}, null, 2);
    const fullKeys = Object.keys(err || {}).join(", ");

    console.error("=== STORAGE FORENSIC FAILED ===");
    console.error("FULL ERROR:", err);

    showDebug("FORENSIC TEST FAILED");
    showDebug("code = " + code);
    showDebug("message = " + message);
    showDebug("serverResponse = " + serverResponse);
    showDebug("customData = " + customData);
    showDebug("error keys = " + fullKeys);

    alert(
      "FORENSIC FAILED\n\n" +
      "CODE:\n" + code +
      "\n\nMESSAGE:\n" + message +
      "\n\nSERVER RESPONSE:\n" + serverResponse +
      "\n\nCUSTOM DATA:\n" + customData +
      "\n\nERROR KEYS:\n" + fullKeys
    );
  }
}

  const panel = document.getElementById("debugPanel");

}

  const panel = document.getElementById("debugPanel");
  if(!panel) return;
  panel.textContent = "=== SAYBON STORAGE DEBUG ===\n";
}

  debugWrite("[" + label + "]");
  debugWrite("window.location.origin = " + window.location.origin);
  debugWrite("window.location.href = " + window.location.href);
  debugWrite("firebase projectId = " + (firebase.app().options.projectId || "n/a"));
  debugWrite("firebase storageBucket = " + (firebase.app().options.storageBucket || "n/a"));
  debugWrite("storage app bucket = " + (storage.app.options.storageBucket || "n/a"));

  if(refObj){
    debugWrite("ref.bucket = " + (refObj.bucket || "n/a"));
    debugWrite("ref.fullPath = " + (refObj.fullPath || "n/a"));
    debugWrite("ref.name = " + (refObj.name || "n/a"));
    debugWrite("ref.toString = " + (refObj.toString ? refObj.toString() : "n/a"));
  }

  debugWrite("--------------------------------");
}

<script>
const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey:"AIzaSyB2aKUdE1NSt0kN332BwTYSX52D0lxj1g0",
  authDomain:"saybon-3e3c2.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId:"saybon-3e3c2",
  storageBucket:"saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app",
  messagingSenderId:"75085012344",
  appId:"1:75085012344:web:0b18581cb0a30c3df47c8d"
};

firebase.initializeApp(firebaseConfig);

const db = firebase.firestore();
const storage = firebase.app().storage("gs://saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app");

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const test = params.get("test") || "prim";

let testData = null;
let current = 0;
let answers = {};
let submitting = false;

let recorder = null;
let recorderStream = null;
let recorderChunks = [];
let recorderQuestionIndex = null;
let audioContext = null;
let analyser = null;
let sourceNode = null;
let waveAnimation = null;

function esc(str){
  return String(str ?? "")
    .replaceAll("&","&amp;")
    .replaceAll("<","&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">","&gt;")
    .replaceAll('"',"&quot;")
    .replaceAll("'","&#39;");
}

function typeLabel(type){
  if(type === "listening") return "Listening";
  if(type === "reading") return "Reading";
  if(type === "writing") return "Writing";
  if(type === "speaking") return "Speaking";
  return "Question";
}

function optionBadge(i){
  return ["A","B","C","D","E","F"][i] || String(i + 1);
}

function renderCurrentSlide(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  const stage = document.getElementById("stage");

  let html = `
    <section data-index="${current}">
      <div class="pill">${esc(typeLabel(q.type))}</div>
      <h2 class="questionText">${esc(q.question || "")}</h2>
  `;

  if(q.type === "listening"){
    html += `
      <div class="audioBox">
        <audio controls controlsList="nodownload" src="${esc(q.audio || "")}"></audio>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "reading" && q.text){
    html += `
      <div class="readingBox">${esc(q.text)}</div>
    `;
  }

  if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && Array.isArray(q.choices)){
    html += `<div class="answerGrid">`;
    q.choices.forEach((choice, i) => {
      const checked = String(answers[current] ?? "") === String(i) ? "checked" : "";
      html += `
        <label class="option">
          <input type="radio" name="q${current}" value="${i}" ${checked}>
          <span class="optionCard">
            <span class="badge">${optionBadge(i)}</span>
            <span>${esc(choice)}</span>
          </span>
        </label>
      `;
    });
    html += `</div>`;
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    html += `
      <div class="writingBox">
        ${q.prompt ? `<div class="readingBox" style="margin-bottom:14px;">${esc(q.prompt)}</div>` : ""}
        <textarea id="write${current}" placeholder="Type your answer here...">${esc(answers[current] || "")}</textarea>
        <div class="helper">Write clearly and answer only what is asked.</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "speaking"){
    const hasSaved = !!answers[current];
    const statusText = hasSaved ? "Recording saved." : "Press start, speak clearly, then stop.";
    html += `
      <div class="speakingBox">
        <div class="helper" style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:14px;">Your answer will be recorded and saved with your test.</div>
        <div class="recordControls">
          <button class="btn btnPrimary" type="button" id="startRecBtn" onclick="startRecording(${current})">Start recording</button>
          <button class="btn btnDanger" type="button" id="stopRecBtn" onclick="stopRecording()">Stop</button>
<button class="btn btnMuted" type="button" id="storageTestBtn" onclick="runStorageTest()">Test upload</button>
        </div>
        <div class="waveShell">
          <canvas id="waveCanvas" width="900" height="92"></canvas>
        </div>
        <div class="recStatus" id="recStatus">${esc(statusText)}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  html += `</section>`;
  stage.innerHTML = html;

  updateProgress();
  updateCenterNote();
}

function updateProgress(){
  const total = testData.questions.length;
  document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${current + 1} / ${total}`;
  document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = `${((current + 1) / total) * 100}%`;
  document.getElementById("backBtn").style.visibility = current === 0 ? "hidden" : "visible";
  document.getElementById("nextBtn").innerText = current === total - 1 ? "Finish" : "Next";
}

function updateCenterNote(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  let text = "Choose an answer, then continue.";
  if(q.type === "listening") text = "Listen carefully before choosing your answer.";
  if(q.type === "writing") text = "Take your time and write a complete answer.";
  if(q.type === "speaking") text = answers[current] ? "Recording captured. You can move on." : "Record your answer before moving on.";
  document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = text;
}

function saveCurrentAnswer(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];

  if(q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading"){
    const selected = document.querySelector(`input[name="q${current}"]:checked`);
    if(selected){
      answers[current] = selected.value;
    }
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    const box = document.getElementById(`write${current}`);
    if(box){
      answers[current] = box.value.trim();
    }
  }
}

function nextSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
    current += 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
    return;
  }

  submitTest();
}

function prevSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current > 0){
    current -= 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }
}

function drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx){
  if(!analyser) return;

  const bufferLength = analyser.fftSize;
  const dataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);

  function draw(){
    waveAnimation = requestAnimationFrame(draw);

    analyser.getByteTimeDomainData(dataArray);

    ctx.fillStyle = "#eef4ff";
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

    ctx.lineWidth = 2;
    ctx.strokeStyle = "#4f8cff";
    ctx.beginPath();

    const sliceWidth = canvas.width / bufferLength;
    let x = 0;

    for(let i=0;i<bufferLength;i++){
      const v = dataArray[i] / 128.0;
      const y = v * canvas.height / 2;

      if(i === 0){
        ctx.moveTo(x,y);
      }else{
        ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }

      x += sliceWidth;
    }

    ctx.lineTo(canvas.width, canvas.height / 2);
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  draw();
}

async function startRecording(index){
  try{
    if(recorder || recorderStream) return;

    recorderQuestionIndex = index;
    recorderChunks = [];

    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const canvas = document.getElementById("waveCanvas");
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");

    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = true;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = false;
    if(status) status.innerText = "Recording...";

    recorderStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio:true });

    audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(recorderStream);
    analyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
    analyser.fftSize = 2048;
    sourceNode.connect(analyser);

    drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx);

    recorder = new MediaRecorder(recorderStream);

    recorder.ondataavailable = (e)=>{
      if(e.data && e.data.size > 0){
        recorderChunks.push(e.data);
      }
    };

    recorder.onstop = async ()=>{
      let saveSucceeded = false;

      try{
        const blob = new Blob(recorderChunks, { type:"audio/webm" });
        const path = `placement-audio/${test}/${Date.now()}-${recorderQuestionIndex}.webm`;
        const ref = storage.ref(path);
        dumpStorageContext("RECORDER PUT", ref);

        const uploadResult = await Promise.race([
          ref.put(blob),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("Upload timed out")), 20000);
          })
        ]);

        const url = await Promise.race([
          uploadResult.ref.getDownloadURL(),
          new Promise((_, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("URL fetch timed out")), 10000);
          })
        ]);

        answers[recorderQuestionIndex] = url;
        saveSucceeded = true;

        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording saved.";
        updateCenterNote();
      }catch(err){
        const code = err?.code || "unknown-error";
        const message = err?.message || "No extra message";
        const serverResponse = err?.serverResponse || "No serverResponse";
        const customData = JSON.stringify(err?.customData || {}, null, 2);

        if(status) status.innerText = `Recording upload failed: ${code}`;

        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR FULL:", err);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR CODE:", code);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR MESSAGE:", message);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR SERVER RESPONSE:", serverResponse);
        console.error("UPLOAD ERROR CUSTOM DATA:", customData);

        alert(
          "UPLOAD ERROR:`n" + code +
          "`n`nMESSAGE:`n" + message +
          "`n`nSERVER RESPONSE:`n" + serverResponse +
          "`n`nCUSTOM DATA:`n" + customData
        );
      }finally{
        if(recorderStream){
          recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
        }

        if(sourceNode){
          try{ sourceNode.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(analyser){
          try{ analyser.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(audioContext && audioContext.state !== "closed"){
          try{ await audioContext.close(); }catch(e){}
        }

        cancelAnimationFrame(waveAnimation);
        ctx.clearRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

        recorder = null;
        recorderStream = null;
        recorderChunks = [];
        recorderQuestionIndex = null;
        audioContext = null;
        analyser = null;
        sourceNode = null;
        waveAnimation = null;

        if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
        if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
      }

      if(saveSucceeded){
        setTimeout(()=>{
          if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
            current += 1;
            renderCurrentSlide();
          }else{
            submitTest();
          }
        }, 500);
      }
    };

    recorder.start();
  }catch(err){
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");

    if(status) status.innerText = "Microphone access failed.";
    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;

    console.error(err);
  }
}

function stopRecording(){
  if(!recorder) return;

  const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
  const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");

  if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
  if(status) status.innerText = "Saving recording...";

  if(recorderStream){
    recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
  }

  try{
    recorder.stop();
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    if(status) status.innerText = "Could not stop recording.";
  }
}

function scoreObjectiveAnswers(){
  let score = 0;

  testData.questions.forEach((q, index)=>{
    if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && typeof q.answer !== "undefined"){
      if(String(answers[index] ?? "") === String(q.answer)){
        score += 1;
      }
    }
  });

  return score;
}

async function submitTest(){
  if(submitting) return;
  submitting = true;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  const score = scoreObjectiveAnswers();

  try{
    await db.collection("placementTests").add({
      test,
      title: testData.title,
      answers,
      objectiveScore: score,
      totalQuestions: testData.questions.length,
      created: new Date()
    });

    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="finishBox">
        <h2>Test submitted</h2>
        <p>Your responses have been saved successfully.</p>
        <button class="btn btnPrimary" onclick="window.location='/dashboard/index.html'">Return to dashboard</button>
      </div>
    `;

    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "Submission complete.";
    document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = "100%";
    document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${testData.questions.length} / ${testData.questions.length}`;
  }catch(err){
    submitting = false;
    alert("Submission failed. Please try again.");
    console.error(err);
  }
}

async function loadTest(){
  try{
    const res = await fetch(`/features/delf/tests/${test}.json`);
    if(!res.ok){
      throw new Error("Test file not found");
    }

    testData = await res.json();

    document.getElementById("title").innerText = testData.title || "Placement Test";
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }catch(err){
    document.getElementById("title").innerText = "Test unavailable";
    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="errorBox">
        <h2>We couldn't load this test.</h2>
        <p>Please check the test link or try again later.</p>
      </div>
    `;
    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "No test loaded.";
    console.error(err);
  }
}


async function runStorageTest(){
  try{
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    if(status) status.innerText = "Running storage test...";

    console.log("=== STORAGE SELF TEST START ===");
    console.log("Firebase app:", firebase.app().options);
    console.log("Storage bucket from config:", firebase.app().options.storageBucket);

    const blob = new Blob(["SayBon storage test"], { type: "text/plain" });
    const path = `debug/test-${Date.now()}.txt`;
    const ref = storage.ref(path);
        dumpStorageContext("RECORDER PUT", ref);

    console.log("Storage ref fullPath:", ref.fullPath);
    console.log("Uploading tiny test file...");

    const snap = await ref.put(blob);
    console.log("Upload snapshot:", snap);

    const url = await ref.getDownloadURL();
    console.log("STORAGE TEST SUCCESS URL:", url);

    if(status) status.innerText = "Storage test passed.";
    alert("STORAGE TEST PASSED`n`nFile uploaded successfully.");
  }catch(err){
    const code = err?.code || "unknown-error";
    const message = err?.message || "No extra message";
    const serverResponse = err?.serverResponse || "No serverResponse";
    const customData = JSON.stringify(err?.customData || {}, null, 2);

    console.error("=== STORAGE SELF TEST FAILED ===");
    console.error("STORAGE TEST FULL ERROR:", err);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST CODE:", code);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST MESSAGE:", message);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST SERVER RESPONSE:", serverResponse);
    console.error("STORAGE TEST CUSTOM DATA:", customData);

    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    if(status) status.innerText = `Storage test failed: ${code}`;

    alert(
      "STORAGE TEST FAILED`n`n" + code +
      "`n`nMESSAGE:`n" + message +
      "`n`nSERVER RESPONSE:`n" + serverResponse +
      "`n`nCUSTOM DATA:`n" + customData
    );
  }
}


function showDebug(msg){
  const panel = document.getElementById("debugPanel");
  if(!panel) return;
  panel.style.display = "block";
  panel.textContent += "\n" + msg;
}

function clearDebug(){
  const panel = document.getElementById("debugPanel");
  if(!panel) return;
  panel.style.display = "block";
  panel.textContent = "=== SAYBON STORAGE FORENSIC LOG ===\n";
}

function dumpStorageContext(label, refObj){
  try{
    showDebug("[" + label + "]");
    showDebug("location.href = " + window.location.href);
    showDebug("origin = " + window.location.origin);
    showDebug("firebase app projectId = " + firebase.app().options.projectId);
    showDebug("firebase app storageBucket = " + firebase.app().options.storageBucket);
    showDebug("storage bucket via SDK = " + storage.app.options.storageBucket);
    if(refObj){
      showDebug("ref.fullPath = " + (refObj.fullPath || "n/a"));
      showDebug("ref.bucket = " + (refObj.bucket || "n/a"));
      showDebug("ref.name = " + (refObj.name || "n/a"));
      showDebug("ref.toString() = " + (refObj.toString ? refObj.toString() : "n/a"));
    }
    showDebug("----------------------------------------");
  }catch(err){
    console.error("dumpStorageContext error", err);
  }
}

async function runStorageForensics(){
  clearDebug();

  try{
    showDebug("Starting storage forensic test...");

    const testBlob = new Blob(["SayBon forensic test"], { type: "text/plain" });
    const testPath = "forensic-tests/" + Date.now() + "-forensic.txt";
    const ref = storage.ref(testPath);

    dumpStorageContext("BEFORE PUT", ref);

    await ref.put(testBlob);

    showDebug("PUT SUCCESS");

    const url = await ref.getDownloadURL();
    showDebug("DOWNLOAD URL SUCCESS");
    showDebug("downloadURL = " + url);

    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    if(status) status.innerText = "Storage forensic test passed.";
    alert("STORAGE FORENSIC TEST PASSED");
  }catch(err){
    const code = err?.code || "unknown-error";
    const message = err?.message || "No extra message";
    const serverResponse = err?.serverResponse || "No serverResponse";
    const customData = JSON.stringify(err?.customData || {}, null, 2);
    const fullKeys = Object.keys(err || {}).join(", ");

    console.error("=== STORAGE FORENSIC FAILED ===");
    console.error("FULL ERROR:", err);

    showDebug("FORENSIC TEST FAILED");
    showDebug("code = " + code);
    showDebug("message = " + message);
    showDebug("serverResponse = " + serverResponse);
    showDebug("customData = " + customData);
    showDebug("error keys = " + fullKeys);

    alert(
      "FORENSIC FAILED\n\n" +
      "CODE:\n" + code +
      "\n\nMESSAGE:\n" + message +
      "\n\nSERVER RESPONSE:\n" + serverResponse +
      "\n\nCUSTOM DATA:\n" + customData +
      "\n\nERROR KEYS:\n" + fullKeys
    );
  }
}

<body>
<div class="shell">
  <div class="exam-card">
    <div class="topbar">
      <div class="brand">
        <h1 id="title">Loading test...</h1>
        <p>One question at a time. Stay calm and work through each step.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="progressMeta">
        <div class="small">Progress</div>
        <div class="big" id="progressLabel">1 / 1</div>
      </div>

        <div class="progressFill" id="progressFill"></div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="stage" id="stage"></div>

    <div class="nav" id="nav">
      <button class="btn btnMuted" id="backBtn" type="button" onclick="prevSlide()">Back</button>
      <div class="navCenter" id="centerNote">Choose an answer, then continue.</div>
      <button class="btn btnPrimary" id="nextBtn" type="button" onclick="nextSlide()">Next</button>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<script>
const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey:"AIzaSyB2aKUdE1NSt0kN332BwTYSX52D0lxj1g0",
  authDomain:"saybon-3e3c2.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId:"saybon-3e3c2",
  storageBucket:"saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app",
  messagingSenderId:"75085012344",
  appId:"1:75085012344:web:0b18581cb0a30c3df47c8d"
};

firebase.initializeApp(firebaseConfig);

const db = firebase.firestore();

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const test = params.get("test") || "prim";

let testData = null;
let current = 0;
let answers = {};
let submitting = false;

/* recorder state */
let recorder = null;
let recorderStream = null;
let recorderChunks = [];
let recorderQuestionIndex = null;
let audioContext = null;
let analyser = null;
let sourceNode = null;
let waveAnimation = null;

function esc(str){
  return String(str ?? "")
    .replaceAll("&","&amp;")
    .replaceAll("<","&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">","&gt;")
    .replaceAll('"',"&quot;")
    .replaceAll("'","&#39;");
}

function typeLabel(type){
  if(type === "listening") return "Listening";
  if(type === "reading") return "Reading";
  if(type === "writing") return "Writing";
  if(type === "speaking") return "Speaking";
  return "Question";
}

function optionBadge(i){
  return ["A","B","C","D","E","F"][i] || String(i + 1);
}

function renderCurrentSlide(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  const stage = document.getElementById("stage");

  let html = `
    <section data-index="${current}">
      <div class="pill">${esc(typeLabel(q.type))}</div>
      <h2 class="questionText">${esc(q.question || "")}</h2>
  `;

  if(q.type === "listening"){
    html += `
      <div class="audioBox">
        <audio controls controlsList="nodownload" src="${esc(q.audio || "")}"></audio>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "reading" && q.text){
    html += `
      <div class="readingBox">${esc(q.text)}</div>
    `;
  }

  if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && Array.isArray(q.choices)){
    html += `<div class="answerGrid">`;
    q.choices.forEach((choice, i) => {
      const checked = String(answers[current] ?? "") === String(i) ? "checked" : "";
      html += `
        <label class="option">
          <input type="radio" name="q${current}" value="${i}" ${checked}>
          <span class="optionCard">
            <span class="badge">${optionBadge(i)}</span>
            <span>${esc(choice)}</span>
          </span>
        </label>
      `;
    });
    html += `</div>`;
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    html += `
      <div class="writingBox">
        ${q.prompt ? `<div class="readingBox" style="margin-bottom:14px;">${esc(q.prompt)}</div>` : ""}
        <textarea id="write${current}" placeholder="Type your answer here...">${esc(answers[current] || "")}</textarea>
        <div class="helper">Write clearly and answer only what is asked.</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "speaking"){
    const hasSaved = !!answers[current];
    const statusText = hasSaved ? "Recording saved." : "Press start, speak clearly, then stop.";
    html += `
      <div class="speakingBox">
        <div class="helper" style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:14px;">Your answer will be recorded and saved with your test.</div>
        <div class="recordControls">
          <button class="btn btnPrimary" type="button" id="startRecBtn" onclick="startRecording(${current})">Start recording</button>
          <button class="btn btnDanger" type="button" id="stopRecBtn" onclick="stopRecording()">Stop</button>
        </div>
        <div class="waveShell">
          <canvas id="waveCanvas" width="900" height="92"></canvas>
        </div>
        <div class="recStatus" id="recStatus">${esc(statusText)}</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  html += `</section>`;
  stage.innerHTML = html;

  updateProgress();
  updateCenterNote();
}

function updateProgress(){
  const total = testData.questions.length;
  document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${current + 1} / ${total}`;
  document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = `${((current + 1) / total) * 100}%`;
  document.getElementById("backBtn").style.visibility = current === 0 ? "hidden" : "visible";
  document.getElementById("nextBtn").innerText = current === total - 1 ? "Finish" : "Next";
}

function updateCenterNote(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  let text = "Choose an answer, then continue.";
  if(q.type === "listening") text = "Listen carefully before choosing your answer.";
  if(q.type === "writing") text = "Take your time and write a complete answer.";
  if(q.type === "speaking") text = answers[current] ? "Recording captured. You can move on." : "Record your answer before moving on.";
  document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = text;
}

function saveCurrentAnswer(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];

  if(q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading"){
    const selected = document.querySelector(`input[name="q${current}"]:checked`);
    if(selected){
      answers[current] = selected.value;
    }
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    const box = document.getElementById(`write${current}`);
    if(box){
      answers[current] = box.value.trim();
    }
  }
}

function nextSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
    current += 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
    return;
  }

  submitTest();
}

function prevSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current > 0){
    current -= 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }
}

function drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx){
  if(!analyser) return;

  const bufferLength = analyser.fftSize;
  const dataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);

  function draw(){
    waveAnimation = requestAnimationFrame(draw);

    analyser.getByteTimeDomainData(dataArray);

    ctx.fillStyle = "#eef4ff";
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

    ctx.lineWidth = 2;
    ctx.strokeStyle = "#4f8cff";
    ctx.beginPath();

    const sliceWidth = canvas.width / bufferLength;
    let x = 0;

    for(let i=0;i<bufferLength;i++){
      const v = dataArray[i] / 128.0;
      const y = v * canvas.height / 2;

      if(i === 0){
        ctx.moveTo(x,y);
      }else{
        ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }

      x += sliceWidth;
    }

    ctx.lineTo(canvas.width, canvas.height / 2);
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  draw();
}

function blobToBase64(blob){
  return new Promise((resolve, reject)=>{
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onloadend = ()=> resolve(reader.result);
    reader.onerror = reject;
    reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
  });
}

async function startRecording(index){
  try{
    if(recorder || recorderStream) return;

    recorderQuestionIndex = index;
    recorderChunks = [];

    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const canvas = document.getElementById("waveCanvas");
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");

    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = true;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = false;
    if(status) status.innerText = "Recording...";

    recorderStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio:true });

    audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(recorderStream);
    analyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
    analyser.fftSize = 2048;
    sourceNode.connect(analyser);

    drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx);

    recorder = new MediaRecorder(recorderStream);

    recorder.ondataavailable = (e)=>{
      if(e.data && e.data.size > 0){
        recorderChunks.push(e.data);
      }
    };

    recorder.onstop = async ()=>{
      try{
        const blob = new Blob(recorderChunks, { type:"audio/webm" });
        const base64 = await blobToBase64(blob);

        answers[recorderQuestionIndex] = {
          kind: "audio",
          mimeType: "audio/webm",
          data: base64,
          savedAt: new Date().toISOString()
        };

        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording saved.";
        updateCenterNote();
      }catch(err){
        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording save failed.";
        console.error(err);
        return;
      }finally{
        if(recorderStream){
          recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
        }

        if(sourceNode){
          try{ sourceNode.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(analyser){
          try{ analyser.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(audioContext && audioContext.state !== "closed"){
          try{ await audioContext.close(); }catch(e){}
        }

        cancelAnimationFrame(waveAnimation);
        ctx.clearRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

        recorder = null;
        recorderStream = null;
        recorderChunks = [];
        recorderQuestionIndex = null;
        audioContext = null;
        analyser = null;
        sourceNode = null;
        waveAnimation = null;

        if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
        if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
      }

      setTimeout(()=>{
        if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
          current += 1;
          renderCurrentSlide();
        }else{
          submitTest();
        }
      }, 500);
    };

    recorder.start();
  }catch(err){
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");

    if(status) status.innerText = "Microphone access failed.";
    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;

    console.error(err);
  }
}

function stopRecording(){
  if(!recorder) return;

  const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
  const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");

  if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
  if(status) status.innerText = "Saving recording...";

  try{
    recorder.requestData();
  }catch(e){}

  setTimeout(()=>{
    try{
      recorder.stop();
    }catch(err){
      console.error(err);
    }
  }, 120);
}

function scoreObjectiveAnswers(){
  let score = 0;

  testData.questions.forEach((q, index)=>{
    if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && typeof q.answer !== "undefined"){
      if(String(answers[index] ?? "") === String(q.answer)){
        score += 1;
      }
    }
  });

  return score;
}

async function submitTest(){
  if(submitting) return;
  submitting = true;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  const score = scoreObjectiveAnswers();

  try{
    await db.collection("placementTests").add({
      test,
      title: testData.title,
      answers,
      objectiveScore: score,
      totalQuestions: testData.questions.length,
      created: new Date()
    });

    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="finishBox">
        <h2>Test submitted</h2>
        <p>Your responses have been saved successfully.</p>
        <button class="btn btnPrimary" onclick="window.location='/dashboard/index.html'">Return to dashboard</button>
      </div>
    `;

    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "Submission complete.";
    document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = "100%";
    document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${testData.questions.length} / ${testData.questions.length}`;
  }catch(err){
    submitting = false;
    alert("Submission failed. Please try again.");
    console.error(err);
  }
}

async function loadTest(){
  try{
    const res = await fetch(`/features/delf/tests/${test}.json`);
    if(!res.ok){
      throw new Error("Test file not found");
    }

    testData = await res.json();

    document.getElementById("title").innerText = testData.title || "Placement Test";
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }catch(err){
    document.getElementById("title").innerText = "Test unavailable";
    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="errorBox">
        <h2>We couldn't load this test.</h2>
        <p>Please check the test link or try again later.</p>
      </div>
    `;
    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "No test loaded.";
    console.error(err);
  }
}

loadTest();
</script>
</body>
</html>

  .topbar{flex-direction:column;align-items:flex-start}

<body>
<div class="shell">
  <div class="exam-card">
    <div class="topbar">
      <div class="brand">
        <h1 id="title">Loading test...</h1>
        <p>One question at a time. Stay calm and work through each step.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="progressMeta">
        <div class="small">Progress</div>
        <div class="big" id="progressLabel">1 / 1</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="progressWrap">
      <div class="progressTrack">
        <div class="progressFill" id="progressFill"></div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="stage" id="stage"></div>

    <div class="nav" id="nav">
      <button class="btn btnMuted" id="backBtn" type="button" onclick="prevSlide()">Back</button>
      <div class="navCenter" id="centerNote">Choose an answer, then continue.</div>
      <button class="btn btnPrimary" id="nextBtn" type="button" onclick="nextSlide()">Next</button>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<script>
const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey:"AIzaSyB2aKUdE1NSt0kN332BwTYSX52D0lxj1g0",
  authDomain:"saybon-3e3c2.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId:"saybon-3e3c2",
  storageBucket:"saybon-3e3c2.firebasestorage.app",
  messagingSenderId:"75085012344",
  appId:"1:75085012344:web:0b18581cb0a30c3df47c8d"
};

firebase.initializeApp(firebaseConfig);

const db = firebase.firestore();

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const test = params.get("test") || "prim";

let testData = null;
let current = 0;
let answers = {};
let submitting = false;

/* recorder state */
let recorder = null;
let recorderStream = null;
let recorderChunks = [];
let recorderQuestionIndex = null;
let audioContext = null;
let analyser = null;
let sourceNode = null;
let waveAnimation = null;

function esc(str){
  return String(str ?? "")
    .replaceAll("&","&amp;")
    .replaceAll("<","&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">","&gt;")
    .replaceAll('"',"&quot;")
    .replaceAll("'","&#39;");
}

function typeLabel(type){
  if(type === "listening") return "Listening";
  if(type === "reading") return "Reading";
  if(type === "writing") return "Writing";
  if(type === "speaking") return "Speaking";
  return "Question";
}

function optionBadge(i){
  return ["A","B","C","D","E","F"][i] || String(i + 1);
}

function getSavedAudio(index){
  const a = answers[index];
  if(a && typeof a === "object" && a.kind === "audio" && a.data){
    return a.data;
  }
  return "";
}

function renderCurrentSlide(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  const stage = document.getElementById("stage");
  const savedAudio = getSavedAudio(current);
  const hasSaved = !!savedAudio;

  let html = `
    <section data-index="${current}">
      <div class="pill">${esc(typeLabel(q.type))}</div>
      <h2 class="questionText">${esc(q.question || "")}</h2>
  `;

  if(q.type === "listening"){
    html += `
      <div class="audioBox">
        <audio controls controlsList="nodownload" src="${esc(q.audio || "")}"></audio>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "reading" && q.text){
    html += `
      <div class="readingBox">${esc(q.text)}</div>
    `;
  }

  if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && Array.isArray(q.choices)){
    html += `<div class="answerGrid">`;
    q.choices.forEach((choice, i) => {
      const checked = String(answers[current] ?? "") === String(i) ? "checked" : "";
      html += `
        <label class="option">
          <input type="radio" name="q${current}" value="${i}" ${checked}>
          <span class="optionCard">
            <span class="badge">${optionBadge(i)}</span>
            <span>${esc(choice)}</span>
          </span>
        </label>
      `;
    });
    html += `</div>`;
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    html += `
      <div class="writingBox">
        ${q.prompt ? `<div class="readingBox" style="margin-bottom:14px;">${esc(q.prompt)}</div>` : ""}
        <textarea id="write${current}" placeholder="Type your answer here...">${esc(answers[current] || "")}</textarea>
        <div class="helper">Write clearly and answer only what is asked.</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  if(q.type === "speaking"){
    const statusText = hasSaved ? "Recording saved. You can play it or re-record it." : "Press start, speak clearly, then stop.";
    html += `
      <div class="speakingBox">
        <div class="helper" style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:14px;">Your answer will be recorded and saved with your test.</div>

        <div class="recordControls">
          <button class="btn btnPrimary" type="button" id="startRecBtn" onclick="startRecording(${current})">Start recording</button>
          <button class="btn btnDanger" type="button" id="stopRecBtn" onclick="stopRecording()">Stop</button>
        </div>

        <div class="waveShell">
          <canvas id="waveCanvas" width="900" height="92"></canvas>
        </div>

        <div class="recStatus" id="recStatus">${esc(statusText)}</div>

        <div id="audioPreviewWrap">
          ${hasSaved ? `
            <div class="previewShell">
              <div class="helper" style="margin-top:0;">Preview your saved answer before continuing.</div>
              <audio id="savedAudioPlayer" controls src="${savedAudio}"></audio>
              <div class="previewActions">
                <button class="btn btnMuted" type="button" onclick="playSavedAudio()">Play recording</button>
                <button class="btn btnDanger" type="button" onclick="reRecord(${current})">Re-record</button>
              </div>
            </div>
          ` : ``}
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  html += `</section>`;
  stage.innerHTML = html;

  updateProgress();
  updateCenterNote();

  const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
  if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
}

function updateProgress(){
  const total = testData.questions.length;
  document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${current + 1} / ${total}`;
  document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = `${((current + 1) / total) * 100}%`;
  document.getElementById("backBtn").style.visibility = current === 0 ? "hidden" : "visible";
  document.getElementById("nextBtn").innerText = current === total - 1 ? "Finish" : "Next";
}

function updateCenterNote(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];
  let text = "Choose an answer, then continue.";
  if(q.type === "listening") text = "Listen carefully before choosing your answer.";
  if(q.type === "writing") text = "Take your time and write a complete answer.";
  if(q.type === "speaking") text = getSavedAudio(current) ? "Playback available. Re-record if needed, then continue." : "Record your answer before moving on.";
  document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = text;
}

function saveCurrentAnswer(){
  const q = testData.questions[current];

  if(q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading"){
    const selected = document.querySelector(`input[name="q${current}"]:checked`);
    if(selected){
      answers[current] = selected.value;
    }
  }

  if(q.type === "writing"){
    const box = document.getElementById(`write${current}`);
    if(box){
      answers[current] = box.value.trim();
    }
  }
}

function nextSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current < testData.questions.length - 1){
    current += 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
    return;
  }

  submitTest();
}

function prevSlide(){
  if(submitting) return;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  if(current > 0){
    current -= 1;
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }
}

function drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx){
  if(!analyser) return;

  const bufferLength = analyser.fftSize;
  const dataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);

  function draw(){
    waveAnimation = requestAnimationFrame(draw);

    analyser.getByteTimeDomainData(dataArray);

    ctx.fillStyle = "#eef4ff";
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

    ctx.lineWidth = 2;
    ctx.strokeStyle = "#4f8cff";
    ctx.beginPath();

    const sliceWidth = canvas.width / bufferLength;
    let x = 0;

    for(let i=0;i<bufferLength;i++){
      const v = dataArray[i] / 128.0;
      const y = v * canvas.height / 2;

      if(i === 0){
        ctx.moveTo(x,y);
      }else{
        ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }

      x += sliceWidth;
    }

    ctx.lineTo(canvas.width, canvas.height / 2);
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  draw();
}

function blobToBase64(blob){
  return new Promise((resolve, reject)=>{
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onloadend = ()=> resolve(reader.result);
    reader.onerror = reject;
    reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
  });
}

function playSavedAudio(){
  const player = document.getElementById("savedAudioPlayer");
  if(player){
    player.play().catch(err=>console.error(err));
  }
}

function reRecord(index){
  answers[index] = null;
  renderCurrentSlide();
}

async function startRecording(index){
  try{
    if(recorder || recorderStream) return;

    recorderQuestionIndex = index;
    recorderChunks = [];

    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const canvas = document.getElementById("waveCanvas");
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");

    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = true;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = false;
    if(status) status.innerText = "Recording...";

    const previewWrap = document.getElementById("audioPreviewWrap");
    if(previewWrap) previewWrap.innerHTML = "";

    recorderStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio:true });

    audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(recorderStream);
    analyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
    analyser.fftSize = 2048;
    sourceNode.connect(analyser);

    drawWaveLoop(canvas, ctx);

    recorder = new MediaRecorder(recorderStream);

    recorder.ondataavailable = (e)=>{
      if(e.data && e.data.size > 0){
        recorderChunks.push(e.data);
      }
    };

    recorder.onstop = async ()=>{
      try{
        const blob = new Blob(recorderChunks, { type:"audio/webm" });
        const base64 = await blobToBase64(blob);

        answers[recorderQuestionIndex] = {
          kind: "audio",
          mimeType: "audio/webm",
          data: base64,
          savedAt: new Date().toISOString()
        };

        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording saved. You can play it or re-record it.";
        updateCenterNote();
      }catch(err){
        if(status) status.innerText = "Recording save failed.";
        console.error(err);
        return;
      }finally{
        if(recorderStream){
          recorderStream.getTracks().forEach(track=>track.stop());
        }

        if(sourceNode){
          try{ sourceNode.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(analyser){
          try{ analyser.disconnect(); }catch(e){}
        }

        if(audioContext && audioContext.state !== "closed"){
          try{ await audioContext.close(); }catch(e){}
        }

        cancelAnimationFrame(waveAnimation);
        ctx.clearRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);

        recorder = null;
        recorderStream = null;
        recorderChunks = [];
        recorderQuestionIndex = null;
        audioContext = null;
        analyser = null;
        sourceNode = null;
        waveAnimation = null;

        if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
        if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
      }

      renderCurrentSlide();
    };

    recorder.start();
  }catch(err){
    const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");
    const startBtn = document.getElementById("startRecBtn");
    const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");

    if(status) status.innerText = "Microphone access failed.";
    if(startBtn) startBtn.disabled = false;
    if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;

    console.error(err);
  }
}

function stopRecording(){
  if(!recorder) return;

  const stopBtn = document.getElementById("stopRecBtn");
  const status = document.getElementById("recStatus");

  if(stopBtn) stopBtn.disabled = true;
  if(status) status.innerText = "Saving recording...";

  try{
    recorder.requestData();
  }catch(e){}

  setTimeout(()=>{
    try{
      recorder.stop();
    }catch(err){
      console.error(err);
    }
  }, 120);
}

function scoreObjectiveAnswers(){
  let score = 0;

  testData.questions.forEach((q, index)=>{
    if((q.type === "listening" || q.type === "reading") && typeof q.answer !== "undefined"){
      if(String(answers[index] ?? "") === String(q.answer)){
        score += 1;
      }
    }
  });

  return score;
}

async function submitTest(){
  if(submitting) return;
  submitting = true;
  saveCurrentAnswer();

  const score = scoreObjectiveAnswers();

  try{
    await db.collection("placementTests").add({
      test,
      title: testData.title,
      answers,
      objectiveScore: score,
      totalQuestions: testData.questions.length,
      created: new Date()
    });

    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="finishBox">
        <h2>Test submitted</h2>
        <p>Your responses have been saved successfully.</p>
        <button class="btn btnPrimary" onclick="window.location='/dashboard/index.html'">Return to dashboard</button>
      </div>
    `;

    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "Submission complete.";
    document.getElementById("progressFill").style.width = "100%";
    document.getElementById("progressLabel").innerText = `${testData.questions.length} / ${testData.questions.length}`;
  }catch(err){
    submitting = false;
    alert("Submission failed. Please try again.");
    console.error(err);
  }
}

async function loadTest(){
  try{
    const res = await fetch(`/features/delf/tests/${test}.json`);
    if(!res.ok){
      throw new Error("Test file not found");
    }

    testData = await res.json();

    document.getElementById("title").innerText = testData.title || "Placement Test";
    renderCurrentSlide();
  }catch(err){
    document.getElementById("title").innerText = "Test unavailable";
    document.getElementById("stage").innerHTML = `
      <div class="errorBox">
        <h2>We couldn't load this test.</h2>
        <p>Please check the test link or try again later.</p>
      </div>
    `;
    document.getElementById("backBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("nextBtn").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("centerNote").innerText = "No test loaded.";
    console.error(err);
  }
}

loadTest();
</script>
</body>
</html>

      <div class="brand">
        <h1 id="title">Loading test...</h1>
        <p>One question at a time. Stay calm and work through each step.</p>
        <div class="candidate" id="candidateCodeLine">Candidate ID: ...</div>
      </div>

      <div class="progressMeta">
        <div class="small">Progress</div>
        <div class="big" id="progressLabel">0 / 0</div>
      </div>

      <div class="navCenter" id="centerNote">Loading test...</div>
      <button class="btn btnPrimary" id="nextBtn" type="button">Next</button>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/9.23.0/firebase-app-compat.js"></script>

FILE: public\features\delf\test-engine.js
